Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee  

Foreword  
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

01)  
Let Us Become Victorious Soldiers of God  
2 Timothy 2:1-13  
<Prayer (I)> Father, please allow this hour to be one in which the life of the original nature that we possessed before the fall is infused into us. May it become an altar of life overflowing with Your love.  
Please allow us to feel the walls of death that have been blocking us with our bodies and minds at this time. Thus, may we receive the gift of resurrection and be able to build an altar of glory, holding up new candles to all the scattered altars. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
Are there those who have wounds in their hearts? Please have compassion. Are there traces left on the body from being seized by Satan? Please remove them. So that we may regain the original form before the fall, we earnestly hope and desire this, loving Father.  
Father, please manifest Yourself with words of power. Please reshape all of us and raise up the work of recreation, loving Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
In difficult circumstances, You have called each of us, so now we will overcome the peaks of trials and difficulties. Now is the time to raise the banner of victory in the remaining practical battles, so Father, please add strength to strength, and power to power, and manifest with the power of resurrection.  
April 8, 1956 (Sun), at the Headquarters Church.  
Let us become victorious soldiers of God  
Please allow the spirits trapped in darkness to be liberated, and resurrect them with the flames of hope. Please allow the flames of Your life, which can illuminate the garden of truth that has been blocked, the world governed by evil, and the ground of Your resentment for 6,000 years, to be granted, my Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
We know that a new history begins centered on You, Father. And we also know that if the standard of history is not placed in heaven, it cannot serve as the overall standard of history.  
Father! You have established us, so please allow us to fulfill a new history and be established as heavenly soldiers of the new era, so that we can build a new garden and return the glory of joy to You. Loving Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
We have found the path that the prophets and sages have walked, breaking through the barriers of battle. We have found the path that is said to be difficult. We have entered a path from which we cannot turn back. We know it is time to fight with independent courage toward a unilateral goal. With our utmost fervor, we must make a decisive stand against Satan and become heavenly soldiers who can charge ahead with the banner raised first against Satan.  
Father, please gather the remaining altars of battle into altars of victory, and until we can gather them into the altar of Your rest and the altar of glory, please protect the path we walk and sanctify the places we stay, so that we can plant the joyful white flag of victory before this nation and 2.4 billion humanity, Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
Father, at this time, a small number of us have gathered to immerse ourselves in Your love. Therefore, please allow us to be submerged in the hidden love of the Father, even if just for this one hour.  
Please reveal the love of heaven and the history of truth that has been hidden for 6,000 years, and manifest the work of resurrection, and allow us to receive the liberation of freedom from our hearts and bodies, so that we can become true sons and daughters of the Father. We earnestly hope and desire that we can face the Father with the song of victory and with the glory of victory.  
This day is a holy day. To the altars gathered on behalf of 30 million nations, Father, please work. If there are dead altars, please manifest the history of life. Regardless of the time, environment, or place, Father, please work.  
Please raise the dormant beacons of life, and allow conscientious children, those who follow the Father, to raise the new flag of life, and let there be many children who can protect the hidden altars, loving Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
Since we have gathered at this time, Father, please sanctify our hearts, and even if there are elements of concepts centered on the self or sinful elements, or unclean dark roots remaining, please manifest with the fiery work of Your Holy Spirit and guide us, Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
Please allow us to fulfill the mission entrusted to us without any shortcomings, and to be able to stand before thousands of millions of saints and the families of that nation with dignity, dedicating our bodies and minds for this one purpose. We earnestly hope and desire this.  
At this time, please protect us so that no one falls under the accusations of Satan from the beginning to the end, and allow even one more life to be moved by the gift of resurrection, to taste the joy of new life, and to receive the gift of new life. Thus, please allow this time to return the glory of the resurrection of new life to the Father, loving Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
Now, we entrust everything to You, so please allow the fundamental work of living life to manifest from the beginning to the end, and let only the will of joy be revealed. We pray in Your name. Amen.  
<Prayer (II)> Father, although we are lacking and sinful today, a small number of us have prostrated ourselves before Your holy presence.  
Until now, You have raised up prophets and commanded through them, and commanded through the Holy Spirit, and commanded through Christ, but we know that You have not yet personally commanded. Please allow the words of Your command that You have not been able to express to appear here. Thus, may Your will, which You wished to accomplish through the Holy Spirit and through Jesus Christ, be manifested here.  
We know that You desire to fulfill the will of joy. Before Your will, we wish to pour out our insufficient sincerity, and we wish to dedicate our inadequate loyalty, and we wish to offer our insufficient bodies, so Father, please extend Your hand of compassion.  
There are traces of Satan's arrows left on our hands and feet, and our bodies are wounded from the battles. Compassionate Father! Please grant Your hand to hold our hands and feet that bear the marks of Satan's arrows, and to hold our wounded bodies, and anoint us with the oil of life, and bind us with the new bandages of resurrection. We desire a word of new encouragement, so Father, please encourage us. We earnestly hope and desire this.  
Please remove all the earthly hearts and all the natures that belong to sin, and allow us to retain only the nature that can admire You, Father.  
Father, now that You have gathered us, please command us. Allow us to find what the center of Your providence is that You wish to seek, and allow us to find what the center of heavenly principles is that You wish to seek.  
Father, please descend at this time. We humbly prostrate ourselves to respond to the words You have given us. We know nothing and our bodies are wounded, but we wish to be dedicated to You, so please accept us. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
At this time, please govern all things, Father. Now, we who have come out before Your will know that we must bear fruit in life, so as the end approaches, Father, please grant us the hand of life.  
Though the world and history may change, we know that Your life does not change, so please allow us to run toward eternal life, the unchanging standard.  
At this time, if there are children who are not worthy before that one standard, please command each one, and grant Your powerful hand, and let them be made in the likeness of the Father. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.  
As we gather before the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit, please remove their subjective concepts and grant us the history of life. May You alone be the center of their bodies and hearts, and the center of the whole gathering, and be the shield of victory, allowing this one hour of joy to be granted.  
From this day forward, as elements of life found, may we form the eternal flesh and blood of eternal life, and create the eternal shield of victory, so that even if we confront Satan head-on, we may be established as children who do not suffer wounds, Father, we earnestly hope and desire this. We entrust everything to You, so please govern us. We pray in Your name. Amen.  
<Words> The message I will deliver today is  
Let Us Become Victorious Soldiers of God. With this title, I will speak briefly.  
We, who are the bearers of the battle and the embodiment of hope, are not a term that has existed from the beginning. It is a term that arose because of the fall of humanity, a term that could not help but arise. In other words, because the battle remains, there was a need for sons and daughters who could bear the fight in place of God.  
God has chosen such sons and daughters because His will cannot be fulfilled without going through the process of battle until a certain time, and for 6,000 long years, God Himself has fought against Satan regarding the earth.  
But what kind of beings are those who must take responsibility for this battle and come to the front lines to engage in actual combat?  
It is not God who fights directly, nor is it Jesus Christ who fights directly, nor is it the Holy Spirit who fights directly. You all know well that it is the saints who believe well with Jesus Christ and the Holy Spirit and God as their background who bear the direct responsibility of this battle.  
This battle must inevitably come to an end. However, even though 2,000 years have passed since Jesus Christ came and went, this battle has not yet ended. Now, we must expand the ground of this battle and create a foundation of victory, and who are the beings that must bear this responsibility? It is none other than us, who are insignificant and humble.  
When we think about this, we can understand that God's hope is not in God Himself. And we can also understand that the hope of Jesus Christ is not in Jesus Christ Himself, and the hope of the Holy Spirit is not in the Holy Spirit Himself, and the hope of the prophets and sages is not in them themselves. It is none other than in us, who are insignificant and remain on this earth today.  
So, if heaven is calling you who are on the earth, what standard is it using to call you? God is calling you based on the entirety of 6,000 years of providence.  
Therefore, you must understand that you bear the responsibility to conclude the history of humanity that has continued for 6,000, or even tens of thousands of years, with victory. And you must understand that the Father is calling you in this way. Furthermore, you must become true soldiers of heaven who are responsible for the times, responsible for history, and responsible for eternal providence.  
It is not Jesus Christ who must directly pioneer the fate of great providence, nor is it the Holy Spirit who must do so, nor is it God who must do so, but it is precisely us who must do it.  
To become heavenly soldiers, we must place ourselves, who bear such a great mission, in a third-party perspective and be able to criticize ourselves. We must consider whether we have become those who can respond boldly even if the Father appears personally and questions us.  
Have we become heavenly soldiers equipped with courage, pride, and conviction to fight for the entirety of providence? If the Father were to ask us this, would we be able to answer without hesitation, "Yes! That is correct"? Heaven is seeking such beings who can respond boldly.  
So, what are the conditions to become such soldiers? We cannot find the conditions to become heavenly soldiers within ourselves. Then how can we become heavenly soldiers?  
To become heavenly soldiers, we must emulate the one who has already appeared as a representative heavenly soldier, namely, Jesus Christ, whom we believe in. The background of Jesus Christ's coming, His life, and all His ideals are contents that can be boasted of against Satan. And to become heavenly soldiers, we must certainly emulate these contents and conditions. You must keep this in mind.  
His words are the same, and the principles of the cross He showed as He died are the same, and the principles of resurrection He left behind are the same. All of these are absolute conditions and laws that we must have in order to conclude all historical battles and become heavenly soldiers.  
We must possess these conditions.  
However, what we must understand here is that even Jesus Christ prepared, worked hard, and suffered for over 30 years until He fulfilled all the conditions that heavenly soldiers must have. It was not accomplished in a day, nor in a moment. It had to go through a long process of trials lasting over 30 years.  
So, what was the path that Jesus Christ walked when He came to this earth? It was to show the conditions of trials and the path of trials that must be overcome in order to win against Satan as a heavenly soldier.  
When Jesus said, "It is finished" on the cross, He did not say this because He had finished everything on the cross. He said this because He had fulfilled all the conditions that a heavenly soldier must have before being crucified. And it means that He had completed all the missions that a heavenly soldier must fulfill.  
Because Jesus was a heavenly soldier without any shortcomings, after He died on the cross, heaven could resurrect Him. Thus, after the resurrection of Jesus, He has been working in heaven, and the Holy Spirit has been working on earth, fighting against Satan for 2,000 years.  
The life of Jesus Christ teaches us.
Now, we who have been called from heaven have a process of trials that we must uphold, which is none other than the path walked by Jesus Christ for over 30 years, and everyone must keep this in mind. 
When we consider the journey of Jesus Christ over his 30 years, he walked through a life of 30 years, passed through a public life of 3 years, and concluded his trials during the 3 days in the tomb. 
It is, of course, essential for each individual to follow the way of the cross and the path of resurrection, but all of humanity must walk this path as well. 
After Jesus Christ died on the cross, he received the grace of resurrection, which was not something that happened easily as you might think. It was not a matter accomplished in one day or in a few hours. The long 4,000 years of history, combined with the heart of God and the heart of Jesus Christ, resulted in the path of suffering he walked for over 30 years, leading to victory. You must understand this. 
While we are engaged in our faith and reading the Bible, we must not translate the Bible according to our own will. Many believers think that the way of the cross was accomplished only on the cross, but that is not the case. You must understand that it was the result of a life of suffering, not eating well or dressing well for over 30 years, that led to this accomplishment. And you must recognize that Jesus is the only begotten Son of God who fulfilled the conditions of the remaining heavenly soldiers. 
Now, we must analyze what lessons the life of Jesus Christ teaches us and begin to repeat the path of Christ's suffering from the start of our faith. You too must go through the process of trials. During the process of Jesus Christ's trials, there will be struggles. And it is not just for 10 years or 20 years, but for 30 years that we must emulate Christ, who fought without fear of death, and inherit the unchanging heart of Jesus Christ. 
What you must understand now is that you yourselves are the ones who must bear the remaining path of suffering and death, uphold the cross, and maintain the way of the cross. 
Since Jesus Christ came and went, the responsibility to protect the fortress of the cross that he built on this earth lies with the apostles. Now, you must understand that the responsibility to protect the remaining fortress of the cross lies with the saints of the last days. 
It is time when we must determine the outcome of the final battle, and the significant question is whether we have become the remaining soldiers who can rise again like Christ, who died and resurrected, and can bring about a second resurrection. 
Even in the spirit world, Jesus is continuing the fight. He is fighting against Satan on behalf of countless righteous saints. The Holy Spirit, who came to imitate Jesus fighting in the spirit world, is the one who must help us to actually fight. In other words, we must become the heavenly soldiers who take on that fight. 
When it is time to resolve the grievances of 6,000 years 
Now, the final battle has begun, and you must understand that the fight you are engaged in is not just for yourselves. That fight is connected to you through the Holy Spirit from heaven. And the purpose of that fight is to expel Satan. 
Therefore, we must become the soldiers responsible for the remaining cross of Christ, crossing over the peak of battle and heading towards our homeland, and we must sing the song of victory. Let us become the victorious soldiers who have resolved the grievances of 6,000 years and fulfilled the wishes of 6,000 years. 
We must become the joyful soldiers. 
The representative soldiers who took on the responsibility of the remaining fortress of the cross after Christ were the 12 apostles. The 12 apostles guarded the walls of the cross beyond death, dedicating their bodies and souls, shedding blood and flesh without hesitation to protect the walls of the cross. Heaven is looking for such soldiers. 
The traces of the blood that the prophets and saints shed while walking the path of the gospel still remain on the walls of the cross. And this land is a land filled with the grievances and blood of our ancestors, a land that still cries out with blood. Who will resolve this grievance? It is us. The death of Jesus Christ is a lamentable matter, but the death of the prophets and saints is also lamentable. You must learn to lament both the death of Christ and the death of the prophets and saints. 
Now we must recognize that the time has come to have grievances. It is time to resolve the grievances of heaven that have been endured for 6,000 years. What is needed at this time is heavenly soldiers. What is required in this era is heavenly soldiers. 
Father! Let the grievances of 6,000 years explode through me! We must become the true sons and daughters of God who can say this. If such true sons and daughters increase among the 30 million people, the path of life for the 30 million will open. If such people become priests to guard the walls of the cross and become fighting soldiers, this nation will not perish. Today, we believers must become heavenly soldiers like this. 
Jesus Christ, who came to this earth and died on the cross, has built a temple of victory in the spirit world and has expanded that temple. As you can see through the spirit world, you will understand that the darkness of the fall reached even under God's throne. Through repeated struggles and efforts, a foundation was finally established after Jesus. Furthermore, the fight to expand this foundation has continued to this day, and the battle against Satan has continued on earth as well. Now, heaven hopes that heavenly soldiers who can conclude this fight will emerge. 
Now we must strive. Jesus Christ worked and fought not only until he crossed the peak of death on the cross during his 30 years on this earth but has continued to fight for 2,000 years. The ignorant humans who do not know this fight… you must appeal to yourselves. Before appealing to the people, before appealing to your family, society, and the world, you must appeal to yourselves. 
You must fight for the purpose as Jesus Christ did for 2,000 years. Thus, we must achieve victory in heaven and on earth so that heaven and earth can respond, represent God's heart, and reveal the original beauty of creation. This is the purpose for which God has governed for 6,000 years and the intention behind sending Jesus Christ. 
What heavenly soldiers must know 
Now we must become heavenly soldiers and guard the walls of the cross. You must discern which rank of soldiers you belong to in becoming heavenly soldiers like this. 
Since the history of the earth unfolds symbolically the history of heaven, just as there are ranks of soldiers centered around the 12 apostles in heaven, there are also 12 denominations and countless regional ranks on earth, similar to the 12 tribes of Israel. 
These ranks have formed over the course of 2,000 years, and you must know which rank you belong to. Just as the world’s armies are organized into small units, companies, battalions, regiments, and divisions, you must know which unit of the heavenly army, organized in a similar manner, you belong to. 
And now you must know what mission you are receiving orders for. 
After going through the process of battle, we must welcome the time when all creation can rejoice centered on one focal point. That focal point is Jesus Christ and the Holy Spirit, whom we believe in. 
What is the ultimate goal of heavenly soldiers? It is to conclude the fight against Satan and receive rewards from God and Christ. It is to achieve victory in the fight and receive heavenly rewards on earth. 
Now the battle is unfolding in every aspect. It is taking place all over the world. The providential will of God is being developed throughout heaven and earth. You must become soldiers who achieve victory in individual battles, family battles, social, national, and global battles, and in the battles taking place in heaven and earth. 
Jesus Christ is unable to conclude the battles taking place in heaven and earth. Therefore, you must become soldiers who protect each department and conclude each battle. As members of the body with Christ as the head, you must achieve victory and, after becoming one in body and heart, worship before heaven so that all things in heaven and earth can respond. 
You must now walk through the bloodstains left by the apostles and take responsibility for the companies and battalions they led. Moreover, you must take on the responsibilities that Jesus Christ and the Holy Spirit bear. 
The ultimate goal of heavenly soldiers 
Heaven does not wish for any remnants of the battle to remain on earth. Because of the grievances that have been bound on earth, we must achieve victory on earth and resolve those grievances so that the fight of Jesus Christ can conclude and Christ can come again. After he returns, what will he do? He will conclude the fight that has been drawn out for 6,000 years and receive blessings from God. It will be a feast where God himself blesses with both hands. The feast of the Lamb will be when the victorious soldiers gather together to receive blessings. 
You must directly receive the words commanded by God, the supreme commander. You must advance to the position where you receive God's commands directly on behalf of Jesus. 
As it is written in Revelation 14:1, "Then I looked, and behold, the Lamb was standing on Mount Zion, and with him one hundred forty-four thousand, having his name and the name of his Father written on their foreheads," you must receive the seal of the Father. 
Until now, you have been guided by the Holy Spirit and have followed the guidance of Jesus Christ, but this is not the entirety of it. You must receive the seal of the Father so that you can become eternal soldiers not only on earth but also in the kingdom of heaven. You must keep in mind that you must advance to that position. 
After you as individuals become such soldiers, you must enable all humanity to become such soldiers. 
You must achieve victory in all battles and become soldiers of Christ, while also becoming the original humans who can please God, completing the ideal of creation. Only then will the victorious song of Hosanna, sung by such heavenly soldiers, shake the whole earth, and the grievances of God against Satan will be resolved all at once. You must understand this clearly. 
There are still battles remaining. Therefore, you must carry out the final assault and become soldiers who can receive God's seal and subdue Satan before God. Only then will the fight against Satan conclude. 
Even if you subdue Satan before the Holy Spirit and before Jesus Christ, the battle does not end. The battle concludes only when you subdue Satan before God. 
To create such victorious soldiers, the Father has endured through the providential history of 6,000 years. You must become victorious heavenly soldiers by recognizing such a Father. 
God's pride, Jesus Christ 
2 Corinthians 8:16-24 
<Prayer (I)> Beloved Father, this day is the day you have granted the grace of atonement to all people. As we go through the process of history, may we not forget the bloody path of your labor and the footsteps of the martyrs who have gone before us. 
On this day, in this one hour, may our worship before you be a time of earnest offering, just as Abel made a plea with blood. May we not gather around the decaying body, but become an altar of sanctification, allowing even a small group of insignificant people to build an Abel-like altar on behalf of the 30 million. 
May we not stand in a position to boast of ourselves as Cain did upon seeing Abel's blood. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. 
Please allow the heart of sincerity and the heart of the plea of blood to penetrate deeply. This land still bears the bloodstains of goodness, and it is a land filled with grief, a land that has the burden of countless years of lamentation. Please allow many children among the 30 million to appear as joyful offerings that can give thanks and worship before you. Please allow this among the 2.4 billion people. 
May a multitude of children appear in every corner who can break down the walls of sin accumulated over countless years and create a garden of joy to bring you joy and glory. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. 
We have lived until today forgetting the hand that has labored for 6,000 years to come to find me and to establish me. Let us not forget that my ability to live comfortably today is not because of my own merit, but because of the countless labor and bloody efforts of the prophets and saints that have led to my being here today. 
As a humble and gentle offering, may we be raised as children who can worship you as a joyful offering. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. 
Father, awaken this sleeping city. Have compassion on this nation that does not know the direction in the darkness. Please quickly raise up the children you will establish and call forth the children you will call. Please allow us to establish a center toward heaven that can represent the whole as a beloved altar. 
May the entire nation achieve victory and be guided to give thanks and praise to the Holy Light. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. 
Father, today a small group has gathered here, so please take charge. Please oversee this. May you discern the center of each individual before you, and may their self-established hearts not stand in a place that begins and ends with themselves. 
Please do not allow them to stand in a place intoxicated with self-satisfaction through their own recognition and ideas. 
May they be allowed to lay bare all their ideas and claims and become humble offerings before the heart of their parents. May this time allow them to feel their shortcomings before the dignified Father and fundamentally offer all that they have to you. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. 
Father, you have gathered these people and established them, and you have already sounded a new bell in this city. Therefore, you must take overall responsibility. They must fulfill the overall mission and take on the overall work, so please allow them to rise above this era and become heavenly soldiers who can stand at the forefront and fight. 
As soldiers who can represent the 30 million people, whether standing before the countless saints or before the angels in heaven, or before the saints on this earth, please establish them in a way that is not lacking. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.
will to fulfill and guide us in this time. May we feel the warmth of Your love and the power of Your presence, allowing us to be transformed and renewed in our hearts and minds. 

As we gather here, let us not be burdened by our past or the weight of our struggles, but instead be uplifted by the hope and joy that comes from being in Your presence. Help us to recognize the beauty of Your creation and the purpose You have for each of us. 

May we be instruments of Your peace and love in this world, shining as lights in the darkness and bringing comfort to those who are lost and hurting. Let our hearts be filled with compassion and our actions reflect Your grace. 

We ask for Your guidance as we navigate the challenges before us, and for the strength to persevere in faith. May we always seek to honor You in all that we do, and may our lives be a testament to Your goodness and mercy. 

In this moment, we surrender ourselves to You, trusting in Your plan and purpose for our lives. May we be filled with the Holy Spirit, empowered to live out our calling and to serve others in love. 

We pray all of this in the name of Jesus Christ, our Lord and Savior. Amen.
establishing a foundation for victory. 

We must fill our hearts with God's love. We need to experience the love of Jesus and the Holy Spirit to feel the love of Heaven. 

Although Jesus achieved personal victory, He only laid the spiritual foundation for victory due to His crucifixion. Therefore, we who must conclude the 2,000 years of history should stand on the spiritual expectations of Jesus and establish a foundation for victory in place of His body.
It is something that must be accomplished. Furthermore, when heaven declares a new word that brings about substantial salvation beyond the dimension of the New Testament, which provides spiritual salvation, Satan will refute it, and we have the responsibility to fight and win against that as well.

Next, under what conditions was Jesus Christ able to receive God's love? Jesus was able to receive God's love because He became a responsible prince. From the time He was born, Jesus worked as a carpenter in Joseph's house, but He made efforts to fulfill His responsibilities. While helping with carpentry in Joseph's household, He lived a life that supported the family's livelihood, but in Jesus' heart, that was not everything about life. He harbored great aspirations while also fulfilling His responsibilities even in small matters. You must not forget that this was Jesus.

Jesus, the prince who took on the overall purpose
Jesus' life was entirely about fulfilling His responsibilities and mission. He accomplished responsibilities that would last forever on this earth. The thirty-plus years of Jesus' life were a life that established eternal and unchanging results, fulfilling responsibilities on this earth. Therefore, as long as the words of Jesus Christ and the gospel of faith in Christ remain, His life will also endure.

Jesus took on responsibilities not only in His own lifetime but also historically. He took on the responsibility for the purpose that God had been working towards for four thousand years. There was no one on this earth besides Jesus Christ who took on God's responsibilities. You must understand that Jesus took on these responsibilities all alone.

While Jesus felt lonely about being the sole bearer of the overall purpose, He also felt a greater sense of responsibility. Thus, each day of Jesus' life was a life that laid the groundwork for fulfilling total responsibilities. Throughout the thirty years of preparation and the three years of practical ministry, and even during the three days of completion, Jesus thought only of overcoming Satan and fulfilling God's purpose on that foundation. His life was lived with a keen awareness of this responsibility. Jesus never forgot this responsibility for even a moment.

Even when He carried the cross and went to Golgotha, at that final moment when all the people were mocking Him and Satan was ridiculing Him, Jesus' determination to bear the heavenly responsibility entrusted to Him did not change. Because Jesus crossed the threshold of the cross with the determination to fulfill His responsibilities, He was able to bring about the resurrection. And because He had the responsibility to restore the disciples who remained on earth, Jesus went to heaven and then returned, relying on God's power to bring about the resurrection.

Even after His death, Jesus was concerned for His scattered disciples, and during the three days in the tomb, He held the intention to protect these disciples forever, which is why He sought them out by the Sea of Galilee after His resurrection.

When we think about it from a human perspective today, it is easy to wonder how Jesus could have done that for His disciples, who lacked responsibility. Although they were the disciples who had rejected Him in difficult times, after His resurrection, Jesus first went to Galilee and began to fulfill His responsibilities. The character of Jesus Christ, who established His disciples as unchanging even when crossing the threshold of death, is the character we should emulate today.

Moreover, we must recognize that He took responsibility not only for the disciples of that time but also for countless saints thereafter, including us today, two thousand years later. The history of salvation has been the history of the whole. Since the will of heaven is to save the whole, Jesus is responsible for all of humanity.

So, what kind of responsibility does Jesus bear? Jesus does not bear responsibility for worldly matters, nor does He bear responsibility for living well. He is responsible for our lives. There are many difficult things in this world, but there is nothing more difficult than this. Because He has taken on the issue of life and death...

Today, believers stand at the crossroads of life and death, where a slight misstep can lead to either. Jesus bears the responsibility of pulling everyone standing on that razor-thin line to the right side. Just as Jesus did during His thirty-plus years of life, and even when He entered the path of death, His heart remained the same at all times. Even if humans do not feel this sense of responsibility and mission, Jesus is still working to fulfill this responsibility and mission, this one purpose.

We must bear the overall responsibility
Then, how should we, who believe in Jesus today, approach Him? We must not become those who place responsibility upon Jesus at all times.

So, what kind of people should we be? Jesus took responsibility for four thousand years of history, for the humanity of His time, and for humanity for two thousand years after His death, and we too must become people who take on responsibilities. We must not live in a way that places responsibility on Jesus.

And we must ourselves say, "Abba Father, we understand the difficulties that Jesus Christ has borne for two thousand years." We should be able to feel sorrow for Jesus, who is still taking responsibility for us and the world today.

Who is this all for? It is for insignificant beings like us. Therefore, we must become people who can bow our heads before Jesus, reflecting on this.

Even as we call out "Lord!" we must feel as if our bones are melting and our flesh is dissolving.

God was finally able to hold onto Jesus Christ, who was willing to take on the purpose of four thousand years, and say, "You alone are the one who must bear the responsibility." Thus, He could believe and entrust everything. In a position to bear the burden of all responsibilities, God could approach Jesus.

In the same way, just as Jesus was established before God, we too must be able to bear the overall responsibility. If the work of taking on responsibility is difficult, we should be able to come before God and Jesus with the heart that says, "Please place that difficult work upon me." We must be able to express that desire through me. Show it through me.

Such people will be the remnant that remains at the end. If such a group does not emerge, where will the purpose of God's only begotten Son, Jesus Christ, who has taken on the responsibility for humanity for two thousand years, be fulfilled? If Jesus, who walked the path of responsibility with His life as the only begotten Son of God, cannot find people who can take on responsibility...

Therefore, we must pray, "Please place upon us the responsibility that Jesus Christ swore before God to bear for the responsibility of history, the reality, and the future." The time has come for us to pray this.

Up until now, we have often shifted responsibility before heaven. But now, on behalf of God's heart, which has been pained for four thousand years, we will take on the historical responsibilities that Jesus Christ bore as the king of responsibility on this earth. Even if the enemy Satan and countless humans do not welcome it, I will take on that responsibility and fight.

Such people must emerge. Only then can Jesus rest in the garden of rest.

Today, at the end of times, the question being asked is, "Who will hear the cry of my life?" But who will hear the cry of life from Jesus Christ, who inherited God's life? Heaven is seeking such people.

Until now, Jesus has been praying at the right hand of God for all people. However, the reason Jesus cannot rest and is still praying is not because He has done something wrong. Nor is it because He is in a position where He cannot stand before the Father. All of this is because of us. Therefore, for the Jesus who has been working hard for two thousand years, you must strive to fulfill the responsibility of life, even if it means sacrificing your life.

Because of Jesus' death on the cross, the responsibility of life remains on this earth. The time to fulfill this remaining responsibility of life is the age of the Second Coming. The age of the Second Coming begins with the emergence of someone who can bear the responsibility of life. He is the one who will take on the historical and future responsibilities of life, and you must fight alongside him in the final battle.

The beginning of the age of the Second Coming
God desires to establish Jesus, whom He loves, so that through the faithful Jesus or the truthful Jesus, He can love humanity. He wants to love you.

Today, when we are told to emulate the faithful Jesus, we should be able to say, "Yes, that is so." When we are told to emulate the victorious Jesus, we should say, "Yes, that is so." When we are told to emulate the responsible Jesus, we should be able to say, "Yes, that is so." If you cannot become such a person, how can Jesus Christ, who has not rested for a single moment until now, find rest?

Therefore, you must take on these conditions that God has established as His pride. And you must become those who fulfill the conditions of pride of Jesus, who has gone to the spiritual world, on this earth. You must become those whom God can be proud of.

First, you must boast of believing in a world that does not believe. And you must boast of having won the battle against Satan. You must boast of taking responsibility in a world where no one else does.

Through this, God's pride will reach us on earth through the Jesus of the spiritual world, and through us on earth, that pride must reach all creation. Only then will the purpose of God, who intended to establish humans as the lords of all creation and to boast before all creation, be fulfilled. Then, at last, humans and all creation will be able to give thanks and worship to God, who boasts. This overall responsibility lies with us.

Today, we are in a very poor state. Our faith is insignificant. Therefore, when humanity must fight against Satan in the future, we must pray, "Abba Father, please give strength so that all humanity can fight and win against Satan. Please allow all of humanity to be able to bear responsibility."

And we must be able to say, "Father, I have fought alone against the entire enemy and won, so please rejoice."

We must show God our appearance of taking on all responsibilities. Through a person who can take on responsibility before countless humans or millions of saints and creation, we can resolve God's grievances toward the earth, and through such a person, God's will can be unfolded. You must understand this clearly. Let us pray.

You have lived. Thus, Jesus Christ has been established as a new center, standing in a position to take responsibility for and save all mankind. When Jesus stood in this position, His heart and body must have been immersed in indescribable sorrow.

Jesus Christ who came to find us
So how does Jesus Christ come to find us today? God established the words to save humanity over 4,000 years of history and announced through many prophets that the Messiah would descend before countless crowds. 

For this reason, Jewish believers have been preparing to welcome the Messiah through the evidence of the words that many prophets have appealed to. This is the history of the Old Testament. Jesus Christ, who came upon this prepared foundation, had to conclude the 4,000 years of Old Testament history as a history of goodwill before God. Therefore, the new words He spoke were not only words imbued with the sorrow of God's 4,000-year providence of restoration but also words that clarified the eternal principles that all beings must carry on their faith journey.

However, despite the fact that numerous Jewish believers should have listened to and believed in these new words announced by Jesus, what must have been the heart of Jesus as He looked upon the crowds who could not believe? You must understand that Jesus appealed with a grieving heart.

Until today, heaven has been searching for just one person, and for a long time, has labored to establish all of humanity, which is trapped in sin. In the Old Testament era, God gave the words of the Old Testament law to the Israelite people through prophets. And to resolve the sorrowful history of 4,000 years, He sent Jesus Christ to announce the new truth. However, because the Jewish people did not believe in those words, they could not comfort God's sorrowful heart, and instead, the sorrowful heart of heaven was further ignited within their own hearts.

For this reason, Jesus appeared before the crowds who were in the grasp of Satan and did not know the direction they should go, presenting the way they should take and teaching them how to live. However, the people of Israel did not listen to those words. Consequently, humanity lost its direction in life, and the altar of God's 4,000 years of labor collapsed. If the Israelite people had united on the foundation of God's words, they would have borne fruit through the words given by God, and God would have embraced them again as His children.

The Jewish people who did not believe in the words given by Jesus
The Israelite people, who were supposed to be a model, did not believe in the new words given by Jesus and could not unite, leaving behind words of sorrow from Jesus Christ. Therefore, instead of standing in the position of a hundred sheep, the Israelite people found themselves in the position of a single lost sheep, and we too are in a similar situation.

We must understand the heart of Jesus as He faced the Israelite people, who are in the position of a lost sheep. To find and establish the lost Israelite people, Jesus cried out with a sorrowful heart.

What we must understand today is that heaven has been working with a sorrowful heart for 4,000 years to find just one person, and afterward, Jesus Christ has been following behind us, inheriting God's sorrowful heart and calling us.

So what process did Jesus go through during His 30 years of life? Jesus prepared for 30 years, hoping for the revelation of God's will. After that period, when He emerged with new words to convey, He did not deliver those words feeling joy, but rather spoke them while bearing the sorrow of heaven.

He spoke many words like "Follow me" and "Believe in me," but the number of people who listened to His sorrowful voice and followed Him was exceedingly small. 

In such an environment, Jesus spent 30 years bearing a grieving heart, and the earnest voice He cried out while He was alive still appeals to you through the scriptures, and even at this moment, Jesus is interceding for you from the spirit world.

Therefore, you must now understand what the content of Jesus' appeals was and find the direction you should go. 

Even though you are in the position of a lost sheep before heaven, if you do not know the direction you should go or what position you are in, thinking that the world will just continue as it is, you are greatly mistaken. 

You may not realize it, but since His birth, Jesus has been calling out with a sorrowful voice throughout the 2,000 years of history, and that call has become your hope.

God's heart and the voice of Jesus
Will you turn a blind eye to this earnest voice calling out? If there are those who cannot hear, they should at least share the same heart of resentment. Is there anyone among you who cannot long for the voice that calls out? You must strive to discern this voice. Even if you have heard the calling voice, if your body is not strong enough to move, you must become a being that can gather your heart toward that place.

For the sake of finding today’s individual who is in the position of a lost sheep, God has labored for not just one day, not just one year, not just a hundred years, but for 6,000 years.

The 6,000 years of history that God has labored to find the lost flock on earth has been a history of heavenly redemption. 

Because humanity cannot hear the voice of God calling out, God has shown Himself through Jesus Christ, who is the embodiment of God, and through Jesus, He has made known His intangible heart, which is the essence of the gospel.

Since humanity does not know the intangible heart of God and cannot hear God's voice, Jesus appeared as the embodiment of God to resolve this. Even though the Israelite people should have come to Jesus, knowing the true will of God that had been hidden for 4,000 years, they did not repent and instead distanced themselves from Jesus.

Therefore, you must prepare to understand the sorrowful voice of Jesus that is being conveyed. To do this, what must you do? Just as you listen well to all worldly words, you must truly have the heart to believe in Jesus, who has appeared before all people on behalf of God's heart and will.

Jesus walked the path of atonement on behalf of ignorant humanity, who had only brought sorrow to God for 4,000 years. You must understand the heart of God that made Jesus stand in a sorrowful place and resolve to make a new determination.

If the Israelite people had been able to discern the voice that cried out on behalf of God's inner heart, they would have easily understood the words that Jesus, who appeared in substance, cried out in sorrow. But what was the Israelite people’s response? They were satisfied only with the words found in the Old Testament, believing that God's final words were all recorded there.

God's sorrow does not end there. When God showed the inner heart of God through Jesus Christ and could not receive Him, the sorrow of heaven could not be connected to the sorrow on earth, which the Israelite people did not realize.

Jesus Christ was meant to resolve the sorrow that God had endured for 4,000 years, but because the Israelite people did not recognize this Jesus, God's sorrow could not be resolved through Jesus Christ and remained as sorrow once again.

Jesus Christ, who came to represent God's will and the 4,000 years of history, could not announce words of joy and left. Therefore, although 2,000 years of history have passed since Jesus, when we look at the 6,000 years of history, we see that God's sorrow and the sorrow of Jesus Christ still permeate the earth.

Today, we must understand this sorrow of God and the sorrow of Jesus Christ, and we must be able to comprehend the words of joy from God and the words of Jesus Christ.

The purpose of Jesus finding us was not always to convey words of sorrow. In the process of laboring to find us, who are like lost sheep, He should not have only spoken words of grief. After 6,000 years of sorrowful words, at the moment when the lost sheep are found, words of joy that can completely forget the sorrow of 6,000 years must emerge.

You may believe that those words of joy will appear from heaven, but that is a great misunderstanding. 

Now we must become the flock that can run toward the Lord who comes to find us, in front of the heart of Jesus Christ, who has labored for 2,000 years. We must not become those who hesitate and fail to run toward the direction when we hear the voice of the grieving Jesus Christ. When Jesus Christ suddenly comes and calls you with a sorrowful voice, you must not shrink back in that moment.

So what should you do? Before you hear the sorrowful voice of Jesus Christ, you must first cry out with a sorrowful voice yourself. 

You must cry out first, "My shepherd! Lord!" until your voice resonates throughout heaven and earth.

Then, when Jesus comes to find you, He will listen to your cry and when He calls again, He will not call with a sorrowful voice but with a joyful voice. You must stand in that position.

We must testify to the sorrowful heart of Jesus
Today, we must testify to the sorrowful heart of Jesus Christ. We should not only mourn the loss of the shepherd but should also know how to cry out to find the lost shepherd.

We must become beings who can take responsibility for the steps of labor left behind by the crying Jesus, so that we can bring satisfaction to Jesus. Today, Jesus is seeking us with a sorrowful voice and is also enduring a life of suffering to find us.

Jesus, who took the place of the 4,000 years of history to save humanity, could not live a comfortable life due to the providence of salvation for all humanity. He is coming to find us after enduring a life of suffering.

As you know, Jesus' life of over 30 years was one of suffering. His life during the 30 years of preparation as the son of Joseph the carpenter was one of suffering both externally and internally.

He could not live freely in a comfortable position like you. It is a great misunderstanding to think that He lived as the Savior of all people. Jesus spent a life of suffering, unable to express all He wanted to say, even being criticized by His stepfather Joseph, Mary, and His siblings.

Jesus' suffering was not for His own sake. He knew that if He did not do it, no one else could find the lost family on behalf of God's heart, which had labored for 4,000 years. With a heart that longed for heaven, He fought through the terrible environment surrounding Him, seeing the struggles of the many who were fighting in dire circumstances, and dedicated His life to achieving the ideal world on behalf of God's mountain words.

From the moment He was born, Jesus was not treated properly and lived a lonely and difficult life until He died, akin to living in the wilderness. While this external suffering of Jesus is indeed suffering, the hidden internal suffering that does not manifest externally is known only to God.

The Israelite people, who should have believed and followed Jesus, failed to recognize the one they should have known but did recognize those they should not have. Among these Israelite people, Jesus longed for the life of His homeland.

The way He ate, dressed, and drank was not for Himself, nor was it for His own comfort. Everything He did was for God, for all of humanity, and for His nation, and the footprints He left behind were also such footprints.

Yet, not a single person understood the circumstances of this Messiah. There was no one who could say, "I understand your heart, I understand your heart, and I will follow you wherever you go to comfort your heart."

Even the disciples, who should have comforted Him, could not console Jesus' hidden inner heart. 

For this reason, Jesus Christ's life of over 30 years was filled with suffering. From the day His public ministry began, the words He spoke were not personal words. They were not for His own benefit, nor were they to establish any power for Himself. They were words meant to fulfill God's will.

However, there was no one who wanted to recognize Jesus, who came with these words and intentions, on behalf of the entire nation. Therefore, Jesus became a target of scorn in the villages and among the entire nation.

Today, you are in an environment where you can hear God's words in a comfortable position. You must not miss this opportunity to encounter God in such a free environment.

The suffering Jesus
In Jesus' time, He had to convey His message secretly, and those who listened had to do so in hiding. That is why the places they went were wildernesses. Yet, even in such circumstances, Jesus tried to bring countless crowds into the wilderness to convey God's words. You must understand the heart of Jesus Christ, who sought to spread God's words to fulfill God's will.

Even though Jesus preached the gospel to many crowds during His life, not a single person welcomed it. No matter how earnest the heart to preach the gospel was, there were many who did not understand. The more Jesus worked to fulfill His mission and responsibility, the more destructive actions were taken against Him.

As He looked upon this, the sorrowful Jesus Christ, who cried out to the crowds all day long in the wilderness, went up the rough path of the Mount of Olives to appeal to heaven once more. His disciples scattered, and He went alone before God to heal His wounded heart and replenish the strength to fight against Satan once again.

You must understand that Jesus Christ spent over 30 years of His life engulfed in the most painful suffering. But that was not all. It is a great misunderstanding to think that Jesus' suffering ended with His 30 years of life. Even today, in the spirit world, Jesus Christ is still in suffering.

The 2,000 years of history has been extended with the purpose of fulfilling God's will, and Jesus Christ, who is carrying out this providential will, is still living a life of suffering even to this day. This life of suffering is connected to today.

So where will this one suffering be resolved? It is not on this earth. The things of this earth are absolutely not the answer. Today, many things that can take responsibility for today...
The necessity to resolve the deep sorrow and toil through the minutes of time.  
Therefore, Jesus manifested the suffering of the historical distance in the providence of eternal life without caring about it. Knowing this fact, you must be able to hold the painful hands of Jesus and comfort Him. Thus, you have the responsibility today to bear the deep resentment of Jesus Christ, who was hated and scorned, and to comfort Him in His suffering.  
But what should you do if you cannot stand in such a position? You must be able to feel the suffering of Jesus in your environment. You should become someone who can analyze the life of suffering of Jesus Christ in your daily life.  
So what sin did Jesus have that He had to endure a life of suffering and pain for over thirty years? If there was a sin, it was only the sin of being appointed as the Savior to save all people before God. You must understand the story of how this Jesus suffered for all people and cried out in anguish for them. We must at least have a heart of repentance toward such a Jesus today.  
In your life, there are also traces of the suffering of Jesus Christ's thirty-year life. If you are to gather this, you must gather all the traces of suffering from His birth in a stable to the suffering on Mount Golgotha, and even the traces of suffering over the last two thousand years since His resurrection. You must understand this overall meaning.  
The sorrow of Jesus did not end with His anguished cries. It did not end even after going through a life of suffering and toil. Today, people think that Jesus' sorrow ended with His death on the cross after a life of suffering, but because of that, His purpose was extended, and His sorrow remains as an unresolved grievance that cannot be resolved. Knowing this fact, you must be prepared to face death and save Jesus from His sorrow.  
54 Jesus seeks us in this way  
In this way, Jesus Christ has worked hard and walked the path filled with deep resentment until today, after six thousand years of history, to find us. He laid down His life and walked the path of the cross, so you must hold onto such a Jesus.  
When Jesus was about to die on the cross, concluding His thirty-year life, He cried out, "Abba, Father…" with deep anguish. The cries of blood from countless prophets and saints who had to be resolved because of the Israelite people after four thousand years of toil could not be answered because the Israelite people did not resolve them. What could repay the cries of their ancestors' blood? There was no way to repay it.  
However, the one who paid the historical price for the cries of blood on behalf of the nation and forgave them was Jesus Christ. When Abel's blood cried out, the countless prophets and saints who shed their blood, the conditions of crying out regarding the torn and blood-soaked land, and the Israelite people were resolved through Jesus. The cries that had been calling out for four thousand years, the purpose of the countless cries of blood from the prophets and saints for four thousand years, were fulfilled through the death of Jesus alone and His resurrection afterward.  
Because of the resurrection of Jesus Christ, the grievances of the ancestors who shed blood on this earth were gathered, and their intentions of resenting the land and demanding forgiveness were fulfilled. Only then could they finally place Jesus at the forefront and worship before heaven.  
We must forgive Jesus  
Jesus, who completed the cries of blood from the prophets and saints sacrificed because the Israelite people could not believe and uphold heaven, what did He leave for future generations? Jesus left the blood of His death on the cross for future generations. Therefore, when you stand before Jesus, you will feel that there was a head of blood in your life as well. This is a repayment for the cries of blood from the prophets and saints, and at the same time, it is a repayment for the cries of blood from Jesus Christ that you must understand. Thus, when Jesus calls us through the steps of the cross, we must seek Jesus through the steps of the cross.  
Now you must realize that the passion with which Jesus Christ cried out with blood on the cross at Golgotha is beating in your pulse.  
Even though Jesus Christ came to find you after laying down the cross, you have not recognized the toil of Jesus Christ who has come to you, nor have you called upon Him who laid down the cross. Jesus Christ, who walked the path of death, who came to find you while carrying the cross, is still crying out for you, infinitely appealing for you, suffering, walking the path of death, and working for you.  
Now we are facing Jesus with the cross in between us, but who will resolve the grievances of this cross? Today, we must resolve it. Before resolving this, we cannot hold onto Jesus Christ and call Him my bridegroom.  
That is why, right after the resurrection, when Mary Magdalene said, "Oh Lord!" Jesus stopped her. And that is also why, from the day Mary Magdalene met the Lord of resurrection, the life of heaven was blocked for two thousand years. Knowing this remaining grievance of the cross, we believers must resolve this remaining grievance of the cross.  
What did Jesus Christ, who came to find us after crossing over the hill of the cross, leave behind?  
Jesus left the terms of bride and bridegroom on this earth. Therefore, now in your prayers, the Lord will appear as the bridegroom. You are the bride, and the Lord appears to you in that form as the bridegroom. When you see the Lord appearing as the bridegroom, you must always think of the price of the blood of the cross.  
Now what remains is what the Lord must find for us, which is the way to abolish the cross and bless all generations, the way to surpass the cross. If Jesus cannot freely hold onto us after crossing over the hill of the cross, we must resolve this one grievance of removing the cross. Before establishing an unchanging standard through my own self, through the altar, and through heaven and earth to abolish the cross, the history of the second coming cannot be completed.  
The light, water, and oil left by Jesus  
What has Jesus, who has come to find us, left for us today? After finding me through a sad life, through a life of suffering, and through the death on the cross, what has He left for us? Jesus has left us the light of life. Jesus came to find us at the cost of His life, and what gift did He bring? He brought the light that can illuminate the dark world. Therefore, when we shed tears of gratitude for the death of Jesus Christ, we come to know the heart of Jesus Christ and understand His circumstances.  
Furthermore, what did Jesus Christ leave for us? He left us water and oil. To heal us, who have been tormented and wounded, what did Jesus leave for us? He left us water and oil.  
Thus, we must light the light that Jesus left for us to recognize our wounds and wash them with water and oil, and we must know that we are sinners and naked and dress ourselves in the wedding garment. It is time for this. In this way, you must light the lamp in your heart, wash your sins clean, heal your wounds, and only after dressing in the wedding garment can you fulfill the wishes of Jesus who died two thousand years ago today.  
Now we must light the lamp of our hearts, wash our bodies clean with water, anoint our wounds with oil, and after wearing the permitted wedding garment, we must worship Jesus without Him needing to cross over the cross. This is what humans must do on this earth.  
Do not wait for Jesus to cross over; you must try to cross over. It is not Jesus who will cross over, but you must become beings that emit the light of life, and then, equipped with all strength, wear the wedding garment that can replace the eternal and unchanging value of light and cross over the cross to hold onto Jesus, saying, "May the Lord rest forever." You must become beloved brides. God desires such brides to emerge.  
Now you must lift the burden left by Jesus. You must inherit the light of the heart from Jesus, receive the gifts of water and oil from Jesus, and then wear the wedding garment... This wedding garment is not just for you as an individual. It should not be fixed in you, but through you, many should receive the light of life, receive the gifts of water and oil, and by wearing the wedding garment, become people who can be brides before the Lord.

<Word> The message we wish to deliver today is "Jesus, who goes and comes for heaven and earth." I will speak for a moment on this title.  
The position of Adam and Eve in the universe  
It is undoubtedly true that God created the heavens and the earth to enjoy His glory. For this reason, He first created the incorporeal world of angels, and then created the corporeal world as a representation of the incorporeal world. And He created Adam and Eve as the center and representative of both the spiritual and physical worlds.  
Adam and Eve were destined to share the fate of heaven and earth as long as they did not change. In other words, they had the fate to move as heaven and earth moved. Therefore, if Adam and Eve changed, heaven and earth would change, and if the center of Adam and Eve was scattered, the center of the entire universe would also be scattered. Adam and Eve were created with the inevitable condition that if the center of the entire universe was scattered, the center of the Creator would also be scattered.  
When Adam and Eve fell, the center of the universe was misaligned, and as a result, the center of the Creator was also misaligned. Therefore, God is in a position to re-establish the center of heaven and earth and to harmonize the created world with that correct center, making the center of the Creator and the center of the created beings one and the same. When that happens, if heaven is joyful, the earth will also be joyful, and if the earth is joyful, heaven will also be joyful. Since heaven is eternal, the earth will also be eternal, and when heaven is immersed in the joy of the infinite realm, the earth will also be immersed in the joy of the infinite realm.  
As long as the fate of the Creator does not go awry, the fate of the created world cannot change. However, due to the fall of Adam and Eve, the center of the created world was disrupted, and everything became misaligned in direction and center. The history to restore this is the providential history of restoration, and through this history of restoration, we have come to today after a long span of 6,000 years.  
Until this time, God's providence of love has been manifested through numerous prophets and sages, symbolically showing love through them, and at the same time, through Jesus Christ, who is the embodiment of that overall love, He has shown the love of providence both internally and externally.  
Therefore, His heart represented the center of the incorporeal world, and His body represented the center of the corporeal world. The Israelites, who should have known this Jesus, did not, and thus they delivered Jesus Christ to the cross. Therefore, you must understand that the entire heaven and earth fell into darkness.  
The purpose of Jesus' words and practical life  
What was the one and only purpose of Jesus Christ coming? It was to establish an unchanging eternal center on heaven and earth, equipped with the heart of the Father who created the heavens and the earth. Jesus Christ came to this earth to establish such a center.  
For this reason, what He spoke was not to establish any personal center for Himself. It was not to establish a partial center in a certain neighborhood of Jerusalem or a certain town in Israel, but to establish a center that could connect to the center of the entire spiritual world, the center of the Creator.  
His actions were not individual actions, and His hopes were not individual hopes, nor was His struggle limited to an individual struggle. The goal He aspired to was to stand as an unchanging center that could encompass all of heaven and earth, transcending all things and reaching the position that represents the heart of God, the Creator. You must understand this.  
You must understand the words of Jesus Christ, the life of Jesus Christ, and the practical actions of Jesus Christ, which were actions that marked the beginning of the new construction of heaven and earth, and His words were those that would bring about the history of re-creation to fulfill that one purpose.  
After a preparation period of 30 years, He spoke during His 3 years of practical life to re-establish the unchanging center of heaven and earth that was lost during the time of Adam and Eve. However, because the people of Israel could not believe the words He spoke, Jesus Christ, who was to be established as the center of the spiritual and physical worlds, was only established as the center of the spiritual world and was not established in the center of the physical world. You must understand this.  
What did Jesus live for until He crossed the hill of the cross? What did He labor for during His 30 years on this earth? Primarily, He labored for the earth.  
However, because of His labor for the earth, the purpose He sought to achieve on earth was to establish a center that should have been completed in one entity, combining spirit and flesh. But due to the separation of spirit and flesh, the body of Jesus Christ, which was to be the center of reality on earth, was harmed. Thus, only the spirit of Jesus, representing the spiritual world, was completed, and the 2,000 years of history since the resurrection has been a period of restoration providence centered on the spiritual world. You must understand this.  
After Jesus died on the cross, He resurrected and, after 40 days of activity on earth, ascended again to the spiritual world. In this way, the fact that Jesus returned, resurrected, and ascended again symbolically shows the history of God's creation.  
In the Book of Genesis, it says, "And there was evening and there was morning, the first day." (Gen 1:5) This indicates that there is a night time. The three days of Jesus' tomb correspond to a period like the night. The 30 years of His life were the daytime, during which Jesus labored to establish His disciples. After this process of labor, His resurrection was like passing through the night and welcoming a new morning.  
The resurrected Jesus labored to set a light on the earth, but He could not establish a light on the earth. Although it seemed that He resurrected to set a light on the earth, in reality, He resurrected as the center of the spiritual world, so Jesus Christ could not remain on the earth and returned to the spiritual world. This signifies that Jesus Christ, who passed through the night period and welcomed the daytime, returned to the eternal world at evening.  
What remains now? What remains is the night period. Because of the coming of Christ, what should have become an eternal morning has turned back into a period like evening due to the death of Jesus Christ, so there is now a responsibility to take on this night period. We must bear this responsibility because we handed over Jesus Christ.  
Just as Jesus Christ established the standard of victory over Satan on the cross to complete the responsibility of this night period, many Christians remaining on this earth today are in a position where they must overcome the hill of the battle of this night period.  
The era in which you can overcome the hill of this night period, following the example of Jesus and resurrecting to enjoy the glory of the new morning with Him, is what we call the era of hopeful second coming.  
Jesus Christ came to this earth and lived for over 30 years for the earth. Because Jesus came for the humanity of this earth, even if the humans on earth oppose Him or say they do not know Him, Jesus must stand in the position of knowing.  
When Jesus went out from the Garden of Gethsemane to the Mount of Calvary, even the disciples who were following Him abandoned Him. When Jesus was crucified, no one acknowledged Him. Not a single disciple said they knew Him. In this way, there was no one who said they knew Him, but because Jesus came for the earth, He established the position of knowing for the humans on earth who said they did not know Him. This is why He went to find the disciples by the Sea of Galilee after His resurrection.  
In this way, Jesus left a path that the humans on earth could know, and after 40 days, He ascended again.  
Now, even when we are in the position of saying we do not know, Jesus Christ is in the position of knowing us, so even if we live in a world that does not recognize Jesus, we must stand in the position of knowing Him.  
Therefore, for the past 2,000 years since Jesus came, humanity has been engaged in the act of seeking Jesus in their hearts. Just as Jesus sought out the apostles by the Sea of Galilee, in order to repay the grace of Jesus who sought them, believers have had to seek towards the heaven where Jesus went for the past 2,000 years. This lifestyle has continued until today.  
So, what did Jesus go to heaven for? Because Jesus came for the earth, what He must achieve is the will of heaven, and even in the spiritual world, He is still working for the will of heaven.  
Having established the standard of knowing for the humans on earth, Jesus went to the spiritual world, and if He did not establish the standard of knowing in the incorporeal world, humans could not remain in the world of knowing. Therefore, for the past 2,000 years, Jesus has been praying before God to establish the standard of knowing from the position where you do not know.  
It is said that Jesus prays for humanity at the right hand of God, but what kind of prayer is He offering? It is a prayer filled with sweat and blood. If humans on earth say they know Jesus, then Jesus, having gone to the spiritual world, acknowledges them.  
If Jesus does not create a position from which He can say He knows before God, the spiritual world that humans can reach will not be recognized before the Father. Therefore, until today, Jesus has been in the spiritual world, praying before God with the effort of saying He knows us. You must understand this well.  
After going through this, how will Jesus come again?
When He comes, He will bring together the affairs of the earth and the affairs of heaven. He will take responsibility for the affairs of the earth and the affairs of heaven on our behalf. Therefore, we must follow the path that Jesus Christ, who died on the cross, resurrected, ascended, and is now in heaven, took until He returns.

At this time, which corresponds to the morning of resurrection after the 2,000 years of night, when the returning Jesus establishes a center in heaven to welcome us, you must feel in your hearts that Jesus is coming towards the earth.

Until now, the form of faith among us believers has been to look to heaven and long for Jesus. This has been the motto and standard of our faith up to today.

In this day and age, we must long for the Holy Spirit, who is working on our behalf for the earth. You must understand this. Countless people have spiritually longed for Jesus over the past 2,000 years, but today we must also long for the Holy Spirit. You must think of this as saints and as humanity. The time has come to long for the Holy Spirit, and the time has come to complete the body of the bride.

Since the Holy Spirit is the spirit of the bride, we must be able to embody the form and shape of the bride. When this happens, Jesus Christ can rest in the spirit world. And by establishing a center in heaven and on earth, we will be able to return to this earth centered around that.

Having longed for the spirit world in our hearts, we must now long for the Holy Spirit, who works within us. Therefore, we long for Jesus, who is the spiritual symbol, and we long for the Holy Spirit, who is the physical symbol, so that the heart that longs for Jesus and the body that longs for the Holy Spirit can become one in us. Only then can the center of heaven and the center of earth merge in my one heart and body. Because of this, Jesus can stand in my place, and the Holy Spirit can stand in my place, and I can represent all people in the will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit.

Now, what meaning will the Lord, who must come to this earth, bring with Him? You must establish the center of Jesus and the Holy Spirit within yourselves. You, who have a living body, must embody the center of a reality that symbolizes the spirit world and the physical world, following the examples of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Otherwise, the entire ideal of God's creation cannot be fulfilled in you alone. The mission of establishing such a center is the mission of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. To establish this one center, Jesus Christ is returning.

What must the saints of the returning age do? How should we uphold this one purpose today? We must not only think about how Jesus Christ went to the shores of the Sea of Galilee to find His beloved disciples. Jesus Christ does not always come to find you. You must become one bride and welcome Jesus Christ.

Since Jesus and the Holy Spirit are the center of heaven, you must establish a standard that allows you to become the center of the earth by uniting body and mind. This is not just a time to long for Jesus. Now, we must prepare the body of the Holy Spirit so that we, as individual entities, can find and welcome Jesus on this earth. You must establish this one center.

Jesus Christ, who desires this one center, has established the Holy Spirit for you and has worked hard for 2,000 years until today. Now you must repay this effort. God has sent Jesus Christ to this earth as the center representing spirit and flesh, establishing a standard that has only been spiritually fulfilled. You must find and welcome Jesus Christ to complete the unfinished part of the flesh. If you complete this in your own body, you can welcome Jesus Christ, who has worked hard until today, into your heart.

Today, humanity must move forward to Jesus, resembling the heart of Jesus Christ and the body of Jesus Christ, resembling the heart of the Holy Spirit and the body of the Holy Spirit, and confidently appear before all creation. You must become someone who can stand before God and boast of your individual self.

And I must become someone who can boast before Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Then, I must also become someone who can boast before the apostles. Thus, standing before the Father, I must be able to confidently declare, "Father, who has labored for 6,000 years! I will subdue Satan, who has been an enemy for 6,000 years, within my own body. Father, from this moment on, please relieve me of the concern for Satan because of me."

Furthermore, I must have the heart to say, "The cries of sin that have permeated this entire creation have all retreated because of me. Father! Please resolve the cries that have permeated heaven and earth through this."

Then, I must also have the heart to say that God has established beloved sons and daughters over 6,000 years but has never been able to love them. Even today, although God wants to love our very selves, He cannot sincerely establish and love us until we believe in that word. 

Therefore, the responsibility of us believers today is... Jesus came to this earth and labored for heaven. Just as Jesus labored for heaven, only those who can stand as the center being representing all creation and the infinite spirit world can participate in the world of glory where Jesus Christ appears with the joy of heaven and earth, and where God, Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and you can live together in the world of joy. You must keep this in mind.

<Prayer> Loving Father, how many times did Jesus wish for the Israelites, the Pharisees, and the Jews who do not believe to repent?

Now, we must bear the words of the gospel that Jesus Christ walked and left behind, and we have the responsibility to fight against countless Satans and return the glory of victory to the Father. Please allow us to feel this in our hearts at this time. Just as Jesus had a heartfelt desire for heaven, may we also have a heartfelt desire for heaven today.

Just as Jesus boldly stood before the gathered multitude who believed in heaven, may we also be children who can boldly stand before the Father’s words of life and truth. 

Please allow me not to boast about myself today before Jesus, and do not let me reveal my circumstances before the Father. At this time, there are many who bow down before you, but please do not let me be ashamed. 

Lead me to be able to take the position of Jesus and to represent the heart of the Father. If it is the Father’s hope that I appear before all people without hesitation at any time in the will of Jesus Christ, please remember these children who are bowing here.
