Lead us to be able to fight on behalf of Jesus Christ to fulfill the Father’s will, and to be saints who are in harmony with the Father’s will. My Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.

Let us give glory to God with the resurrection, just as Jesus did.
It is not just a message that cries out only for the people who do not believe. It is a message for all humanity. Jesus was prepared to die for God. He knew that the remaining path was a fateful road that could not be avoided. He recognized that fallen humanity had not devoted their hearts, characters, and intentions to God at any point in history. Knowing this, Jesus boldly stepped forward and cried out.

"Love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your mind." He spoke these words with confidence. You should not understand this single statement as something that applies only to you.

What does this one statement represent? Jesus deeply felt God's sorrowful inner heart that permeated the 4,000 years of history. He felt the responsibility to serve God and realized that at any moment, he must become a representative who devoted his heart, life, and will in a way that had not been done in the 4,000 years of history. This was reiterated here.

The glory of heaven was to be manifested as the glory of Jesus, the glory of Jesus was to be manifested as the glory of all people, and the glory of all people was to reach all of creation. However, because Jesus was separated from the people, the glory of resurrection and thanksgiving that was achieved in Jesus alone has remained as the hope of humanity today.

Jesus appeared as the embodiment of God's glory. He was a being who devoted his heart, character, and will for God, the embodiment of victory that had not existed in the historical process. Therefore, you must understand that God's heart is accumulated in Jesus alone. Furthermore, you must recognize that before Jesus devoted his heart, God had already devoted His heart. Before Jesus devoted his will, God had already devoted His will. And before Jesus devoted his character, God had already devoted His character. In this way, Jesus appeared as the embodiment of the gospel and a mediating existence.

Therefore, this truth of Jesus is not merely a message felt from the side, but a message through the ideal of human creation, a message established as a glory ideal that can elevate the value of the whole, and a message that reveals the hidden heart of the Father. You must understand this.

Today, you should not think that the words spoken by God were only for His own love. And when Jesus spoke such words, he thought that he must now concretely fulfill the purpose for which God had worked hard to establish Himself. Just as God had done everything for Jesus, humanity has the responsibility to do everything for God, a responsibility that has yet to be fulfilled.

Therefore, we must now honor God with all our hearts, all our intentions, and all our characters, and we must recognize that God Himself first came to us with all His heart, all His will, and all His character.

What kind of heart did God have toward humanity over the 4,000 years? He did not come with a heart to serve Himself. Although humanity deserved to die and to suffer, God walked the 4,000-year historical path of patience toward humanity and fought the battle of discernment against Satan with all His will over those 4,000 years.

You must understand that God has endured, fought, and loved with an unchanging heart of love for 4,000 years.

Jesus, who appeared before such a God, devoted His heart in order to establish God's nation centered on the Israelite people. Therefore, the 30 years of Jesus' life was a period of sacrifice in which He devoted His heart. During those 30 years, He did not reveal Himself before the people but sought to empathize with the heavenly heart that had endured for 4,000 years.

Thus, Jesus felt the facts related to Satan in the 4,000-year historical process and testified to them internally in the spirit world. Furthermore, He had the responsibility to reveal the secrets of heavenly principles hidden within the 4,000 years of history, to fulfill the reality of God's inner patience, and to establish the external reality over His 30 years of life.

Therefore, you must understand that the more difficult the situation Jesus faced, the more He was in a position to seek His own self, yet He could not think of seeking it. Jesus felt the one heart with which God had endured for 4,000 years to find Himself, the heart that endured to find each individual human being, and He prepared for over 30 years to manifest that heart as a reality.

Until this time, God has not justified Himself to anyone. He could not justify Himself to all people, nor to the enemy Satan. Because Jesus was trying to empathize with God's entire heart, He endured without justifying Himself to anyone, even in a lonely position. You must emulate this life of Jesus' endurance.

However, God endured for Jesus, and Jesus did not endure for Himself, but for the Father. In other words, Jesus felt that He was walking the path of labor to find Himself, not for His own sake but for God's sake.

In this way, because Jesus endured for over 30 years, having left Himself behind for God, He surpassed the endurance of Satan. Satan has struggled to destroy the path that God has endured for 4,000 years. However, knowing that there was a patience of the Father that exceeded Satan's endurance, Jesus believed in that Father and endured like the Father, thus becoming the embodiment of patience.

In this way, standing on the expectation of God's heart that had endured for 4,000 years, Jesus fought against Satan with patience and won. However, when He could not establish the foundation for a substantial victory, the heart of God that had endured for 4,000 years would be destroyed.

Jesus, who overcame Satan with the heart of patience, faced situations in which He could not endure, yet He endured because He held onto God's will. He also endured in a position where Satan could not endure and upheld God's will, and because He was established as a symbol of those who endure, Jesus became the protagonist who could fight against Satan.

God walked the bloody path of history for 4,000 years to find Jesus alone. And even as humanity struggled to fulfill their personal desires, God walked the historical path of battle for humanity. In this way, God fought against Satan for 4,000 years, but He did not fight centered on Himself.

However, what Satan has desired until today is for his own glory. Until now, he has fought against God centered on himself. But God did not fight for Himself. The purpose of God's battle was for the miserable humanity trapped in Satan's embrace and to elevate Jesus through the chosen people.

So, what kind of being did Jesus appear as? He appeared as the embodiment of victory, the reality that won the battle against Satan over 4,000 years. Jesus came to this earth as the protagonist of the battle on behalf of God. Therefore, the path of Jesus' three years of public life was the path of responsibility to establish the standard of victory externally, inheriting the internal standard of victory that God had set.

During these three years of public life, Satan fought against Jesus for his own victory but was defeated, so he mobilized the people to fight against Jesus again.

However, during the three years of public life, Jesus never fought centered on Himself, no matter how difficult the battle was. Jesus said that He acted by seeing what the Father was doing. As the embodiment of God's battle, He walked the path of public life for three years, revealing God's inner heart. Jesus did not engage in a battle to justify Himself.

Just as God could not justify Himself for the labor He had undertaken over 4,000 years, Jesus did not justify Himself before all people in the position of fighting against Satan. Jesus upheld God with an unchanging heart regarding the labor of providence that God had undertaken for 4,000 years.

Realizing this one fact, that God's will was manifested through the battle of providence, Jesus expanded the battle to fulfill the entire will that God had established internally. In the battle between Jesus and Satan, while Satan fought for himself, Jesus fought for heaven. Here, the standard of victory was established.

So, what was the reason for Satan's defeat? It was because he fought for himself. The purpose of Satan's battle was for himself. However, Jesus placed the purpose of the battle in heaven. And because Jesus fought with the unwavering heart of God, promising not to change until the end, He established the standard of victory. Just as God devoted His heart, will, and character, Jesus also showed such an attitude before humanity.

Thus, Jesus was able to inherit God's inner character, enduring all difficulties and sorrows while loving, receiving God's heart. Therefore, wherever Jesus was, He fought against Satan as the embodiment of God's will and love.

In the process of fighting against Satan, Jesus understood that when Satan attacked centered on his own purpose, the impact would not only affect Jesus but also reach God. Therefore, no matter what difficulties He faced, Jesus endured as God had endured for Him and as God had endured for all humanity, and as God had fought against Satan throughout the history of providence, Jesus fought against Satan while enduring alone for over 30 years. 

Thus, until the moment of His death on the cross, Jesus' life was a life that practically embodied God's love. However, the path of His life, the path in which He practiced God's love, was a trial process walked while fighting against Satan.

So why did God allow Jesus to be handed over to Satan and die on the cross? It was not because God did not love Jesus. Do you know to what extent God loved Jesus? You must understand that God's greatest love is received in a place that transcends death. Therefore, you must have a heartfelt desire to overcome even the peak of death to receive the love of Jesus, who came on behalf of God. Only then will Satan be compelled to submit.

For 4,000 years, God alone looked at the entire world with sorrow, worry, and labor, but with the establishment of Jesus on earth, a new battle against Satan centered on Him began. Thus, Jesus forgot everything about Himself and fought for God, and even in the moment of death, because He did not carry the desire for Himself, He was able to manifest the power of resurrection. Today, we too must go through such a victorious process like Jesus.

Jesus possessed eternal life from God and devoted everything to manifest God's glory. He offered Himself as a sacrifice for sinful humanity. We must recognize the love of Jesus, who prayed for humanity to the point of forgetting even what Satan opposes.

Because Jesus manifested a love that could not be shown in the world of Satan, Satan had no choice but to submit before His love. Although Satan had his own purpose, he felt ashamed through Jesus. Thus, due to the cross, not only did God, who had been providentially working for 4,000 years, begin to feel sorrow, but humanity also began to feel sorrow, and Satan too began to feel sorrow. You must understand this.

It was not only God and humanity who mourned the death of Jesus. Satan also mourned the death of Jesus' love. Therefore, as Satan's sorrow increases, the fruits of Jesus' love will multiply.

Through the victory of the cross that demonstrated His love, Jesus established an unchanging connection with God, who had been providentially working for 4,000 years, and became the embodiment of unchanging victory and unchanging love. Because Jesus became one with God on behalf of heaven, earth, and humanity, Jesus Christ could not change as long as God did not change.

God sought to manifest glory for 4,000 years, but His purpose was not fulfilled until Jesus was established. Therefore, Jesus sought to manifest that purpose on earth through humanity. He was to appear as the evidential reality of God's 4,000-year providence, but due to the cross, that purpose was trampled by Satan.

However, Jesus, as the eternal embodiment of God, showed the glory of God that had been providentially worked for 4,000 years, and that glory was the glory of resurrection. You must understand this.

The resurrection was the first to represent the glory of heaven in the 4,000-year history and was the glory of victory over the battle with Satan that lasted for 4,000 years. Because Jesus showed this victorious standard both spiritually and substantially, God raised the dead Jesus again to unfold a new providence. By being nailed to the cross, Jesus took on the responsibility of the 4,000-year providential history, took on the responsibilities of His ancestors, and went to heaven to represent the glory of heaven.

In this way, Jesus came to fulfill the inner glory of God on earth, that is, to manifest God's complete glory. This is because complete glory can only be achieved when internal and external glory are combined. Jesus came to fulfill this mission.

For God's glory to be fully realized, the only begotten Son Jesus, who came as the embodiment of God's internal glory, must not be separated from the Jewish people but must become one, so that the internal glory of God within Jesus would become the glory on earth. However, because Jesus, who was to take on the 4,000-year providential history and realize God's glory on earth, was crucified due to the disbelief of the Jews, the internal glory of heaven became spiritual glory.

Therefore, Jesus ascended having achieved incomplete glory.
After ascending, Jesus is engaged in the heavenly battles that God has been fighting against Satan for 4,000 years, the true battle to restore humanity, the battle of providence to fulfill His will, and the battle of love on behalf of the Holy Spirit. In other words, Jesus has gone to the spiritual world and is fighting on behalf of God, taking over the battles that God has been waging.

So, where must Jesus Christ, who has represented humanity and all creation before God, who has been working for 4,000 years, truly achieve victory? It is none other than on this earth.

Let us fulfill God's will for unity through love.
The title of the message I want to deliver today is "Let Us Fulfill God's Will for Unity in Love." I will speak briefly on this topic.

God's hope in raising prophets
Because God's will was not fulfilled due to Adam's fall, the restoration providence has been repeated throughout history until today.

God's original intention was for humanity to live in harmony with one love centered on one will, enjoying God's love throughout heaven and earth, and establishing that love as the center of actual life, living as one. However, due to the fall of Adam and Eve, God's love remained only as God's love. In other words, the love that should have been related to humanity could not relate to humanity and became distant from humanity and all creation.

Thus, God has been working through history for 6,000 years, hoping for that day when all creation can enjoy the love centered on the love He wishes to establish. However, the ideal of God's love has not yet been unified with all creation, and the hopeful love that must be sought remains as it is. Therefore, God has been working tirelessly to fulfill that will.

Throughout the ages since the fall of humanity, God has sought to find a heart that can believe in and love humanity, and has been working for a long time, but has not yet achieved that.

When we reflect on the history of God's providence, we can see that God sought to establish an unchanging standard of hope, ideals, and love for humanity by raising one person, Abraham. Only when the day comes when this will of God is fulfilled, when such a center of love is established, can a relationship between God and humanity be formed. Based on that relationship, God can enjoy a new ideal, which is why He chose and raised Abraham. However, because Abraham could not establish the center of love, God has been paving the way to establish the will of heavenly love until the time of Jesus.

Therefore, the 4,000 years leading up to Jesus were a period in which God needed to establish a substantial being that fulfilled His hope, faith, and love in the overall providence. If such a being were not established, God's hope, faith, and love would remain separated, and there would be no unity at any point in history. Thus, God first laid the foundation of hope. Then, on that foundation, He sought to lay the foundation of faith, and on that foundation of faith, He sought to lay the foundation of love. Ultimately, He aimed for the day when all of this could be presented as a substantial embodiment of hope, faith, and love before heaven and earth. However, if that day does not come, the ideal of unity centered on God's love cannot be achieved on this earth.

To establish that day, God has worked through 4,000 years of providence, starting with Abraham, passing through Moses, and reaching John the Baptist, dividing the history of providence into three stages while laying the foundation of hope. The one who appeared as a substantial being on that foundation of hope was none other than Jesus Christ. Jesus Christ was the substantial being that God had hoped for over 4,000 years, and thus He was the total embodiment of God's hope.

So, what did Jesus, as that embodiment, sow on this earth? It was the gospel of the New Testament established through the path of righteousness, that is, the gospel of faith. Since then, a history of 2,000 years has passed centered on this gospel of faith.

Now, who is the being that will appear as the substantial embodiment of love, representing heaven and earth on the foundation of this gospel of faith? He is the returning Lord you must recognize. So, what does God intend to do in the age of the Second Advent? You must understand that the purpose of God's 6,000-year providential history is to sow a seed of life on the foundation of faith that has been laid until now, centered on the returning Lord.

<Word> The title I wish to speak on based on the scripture read is "Let Us Seek the World of God's Dominion." I will speak briefly on this topic.  
The task of seeking the Lord God of dominion  
All creation made by God in six days has remained in a sad and difficult position without acknowledging God as the Lord of dominion. And unexpectedly, Satan has been ruling over all creation in place of the Creator God. If He has dominion over the entire created world, you too will stand in the God-like position and be able to govern all things. If you cannot establish such a self, you cannot claim to possess God.  
All the sorrows and deaths on this earth today stem from the fact that we have lost God. And because we have lost God, Satan has taken on the role of master. Originally, humanity was to acknowledge God as the sole master based on the principles of creation, but due to the fall, we have made Satan our master instead of God.  
Now, you have a fateful responsibility to reclaim the loving God, and who is it that stands in the way of that path? Who opposes the intention of acknowledging God as the main character in this created world? It is Satan, who instills sin in your hearts today.  
Therefore, you must uproot the roots of sin that are embedded in your hearts, and if you cannot defeat Satan, who has fought against heaven for 6,000 years on behalf of all people, you cannot establish God's world on this earth.  
Then, what kind of freedom are you seeking in your hearts? If you do not seek God, you become a servant of Satan. Therefore, if you do not possess God and instead possess Satan, you become a traitor against the principles of heaven. You must understand this.  
What is the reason God has taught us the principles of heaven? It is to provide a means to seek God and to know God. And the path He has taken to teach us that means is the 6,000 years of historical providence.  
Today, you know through faith that God is real, and all of our members know well that God's nature is manifested as the central character of all creation. However, it is essential that the God you know becomes yours. You must establish an unbreakable relationship with God.  
If that happens, whether you run east or west, north or south, or whatever process you are in, as long as God does not change, the ownership you have over God will not change. If you cannot stand in such a position, God's demands and hopes for you will remain unfulfilled and you will be in an incomplete position. If that happens, there will be conditions for Satan to accuse you, and God's sorrow will remain.  
What must we do as humans in this position today? First, we must escape from Satan's accusations. Thus, we must meet the day when we can testify, just like Jesus, that we are the children of God, qualified to possess God and to establish a unified relationship with Him.  
If we cannot restore such a day, you must understand that you cannot stand before the God who governs all creation as the master of all things.
As humanity fell, not only did we lose God, but we also lost our original nature. When I analyze myself, I realize that in losing God, I also lost my original heart. What you all need to rely on is your heart. If you cannot freely control your own heart, you cannot possess God, and God cannot establish a relationship with you.

When your heart creates an eternal standard of relationship with God, you can possess God, and God can freely govern your heart. Therefore, just as the hearts of God and Jesus become one, today you must enter a position where your heart is united with Jesus’ heart and establish a unified relationship with God’s heart. If you cannot stand in such a position, the conditions for Satan's accusations will remain in your heart.

Originally, humans were meant to stand in the position of the second God by living according to the desires of their hearts within the will that God requires, thereby representing God's overall ideology. However, due to the fall, humans lost the nature of their hearts that could do so, and today, humanity must walk the path of sorrow, needing to find this nature of the heart.

Therefore, we must purify our hearts through Jesus Christ. In serving God with all our hearts, we should not only live with sincerity at specific times and seasons. This must be established as an unchanging system in the future and become a fundamental principle leading towards the heavenly path.

Jesus, who possessed God

9) The Responsibility of the Rooted Ones
Genesis 18:22-19:12, Isaiah 6:11-13

<Word> The title of the message I want to share with you at this time is "The Responsibility of the Rooted Ones." When we look at the biblical passage in Isaiah 6:11 and following, it is written that even if a tenth remains, it will be consumed, but just as the stump of the night tree and the oak tree remains after being cut down, the holy seed is the stump of the earth. Here, God repeatedly mentions that if there is a remaining root, He will cause new shoots to sprout from that root and start a new work.

Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, were to be an eternal, unchanging root of heaven and earth, fulfilling the hopes and ideals of all humanity, but due to their fall, that fundamental root was cut off and uprooted, and moved to the world of Satan, as you well know.

The Center of God's Providence
Therefore, the central point of God's providence that has been unfolding until today was to re-establish that fundamental root, which could be the root of human happiness, the root of ideals, the root of life, and the root of love, through Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden.

Thus, although many prophets and sages who have upheld the purpose of providence did not fully understand the circumstances of heaven's providence, their efforts were to lay the foundation to meet that lost root as an unchanging reality.

So, after 4,000 years since the beginning of the providential history, the one who was to re-establish the root that was lost in the Garden of Eden was none other than Jesus Christ, whom you believe in.

In other words, the mission of Jesus Christ, who came to this earth, was to establish a form of God's vineyard on the fallen earth, which God could freely manage based on this root that would remain forever. This was God's purpose in sending Jesus Christ to this earth.

You must understand that before Jesus appeared, there was a long history of countless prophets and sages who shed tears of blood, centered on the will of heaven, for 4,000 years since the providence of heaven began.

There was the providential will representing tribes, nations, and the world, and there was the providential will representing history. You must not forget that there was a foundation of the efforts of many prophets and sages who could become the root elements as they passed through each region and environment representing that providential will.

And the one who was sent to complete the root that could be established as an individual, to complete the root that could be established as a nation, and to complete the root that could be established as a world was none other than Jesus.

What we who believe in Jesus today must understand is that all the efforts of Jesus' 30 years of life and all the efforts of the 2,000 years of history since His death represent the world. And until the root He completed is established before God, you must not forget the efforts of the prophets and sages who fought against enemies and represented the hidden root behind the scenes of history.

The Hidden Life of Abraham
The historical figure who enabled Jesus to be established as a completed being was Abraham. 

Abraham was a possessor of a hidden personality who did not betray heaven even in an environment where others did not recognize him, that is, in a nation captured by the realm of Satan, where he could betray the will of heaven. Just like Abraham, who was a hidden root, overcame all circumstances even when the times were evil, history was chaotic, and the environment was turbulent, he appealed with a sorrowful heart toward the collapsing Sodom and Gomorrah.
Even if they are bad and evil, it is human nature to boast about whatever they possess. Abraham, while holding the great providence promised in his heart to uphold God's will over a long time, lived a life of hidden effort, overcoming all kinds of persecution and humiliation to establish an unwavering standard as a root that was firmly planted, without revealing this fact and only hoping as a single root that, no matter who touched it or tried to uproot it, would remain steadfast.

In this way, Abraham not only established his unchanging hope before heaven but also became a seed sown for the sake of all mankind on earth, including even wicked nations, with a heartfelt desire to hold onto this standard and not change when the day came to establish an unchanging hope that could turn them back to heaven.

The cities of Sodom and Gomorrah were places deserving of God's judgment and punishment, completely unrelated to where Abraham was. However, Abraham, regardless of whether the people of Sodom and Gomorrah knew the will of heaven or not, felt a responsibility that he could not bear and thus lamented and worried about Sodom and Gomorrah day and night. This inner sentiment of Abraham is reflected in the words written here.

In today's time, at the end of 6,000 years of history, if you are sleeping comfortably, wearing nice clothes, and eating delicious food, it is not because you are so great. If you think that way, it will be a big problem.

The reason the world can sustain itself even now is because there are people behind the scenes who are hidden roots, building altars of tearful appeals. You have a mission to inform everyone of this fact.

If there had been a group of people in Sodom and Gomorrah who knew that Abraham's earnest prayer was reaching heaven and having a dialogue with God, and if there had been even a few righteous people among them who recognized Abraham, he would have earnestly appealed to God, presenting conditions to avert the judgment that was to fall upon Sodom and Gomorrah. If there had been even a few righteous people, Abraham could have appealed to God, saying, "Father, is it not your will to judge the righteous and the wicked together in fire?" 

However, when Abraham felt that he alone was praying on behalf of Sodom and Gomorrah, his sorrow was indescribably great. You must understand the responsibility of those who are rooted.

So, do you know where the reason lies for Abram becoming Abraham? 

You must not forget that Abraham had a hidden standard where he risked his life for his people rather than caring for his own happiness and safety.

The reason Abraham could become the ancestor of faith was that he played the role of a hidden root that had not appeared on earth, established before heaven's providence, just like Abraham. In other words, even if everything else in the providential history was bent, there was someone like Abraham who could demonstrate an unchanging faith toward heaven, allowing Jesus Christ to be born on that foundation.

You should reflect on yourself while comparing yourself to Abraham, who was chosen to be the ancestor of faith from Abram (meaning "great father") to Abraham (meaning "father of many nations"), and recognize that he went through a path of great effort that others do not know. 

Just as Abraham built an altar of hidden roots for Sodom and Gomorrah, you too should have the burning heart of Abraham, who earnestly appealed and prayed for the people of his land and its inhabitants. You must never forget that you should inherit the faith's expectations, the hidden roots that were established through Abraham's efforts.

The family of Abraham, the ancestor of faith, received the promise of being a channel of blessing, which took shape through Isaac and Jacob and expanded to a global scale through Moses and Jesus. If Abraham had not had that fervent loyalty and faith before heaven, there would have been no connection on this earth that could link heaven and humanity.

Today, everyone wants to show off what is good for them. They want to reveal and boast about it. However, those who try to reveal and inform others may fulfill the responsibility of a branch, but they cannot fulfill the responsibility of a root.

Do you know what the hidden secret was that allowed Abraham to become the ancestor of faith? It was because he had an intense longing for heaven and a heart for the earth, which enabled him to have a broad and deep connection with the heavenly Father, allowing him to become the ancestor of faith.

Moses was also like this. Before Moses was established before the nation, there was a period of 40 years of hidden effort in the palace as a hidden root. During his time in the luxurious palace, Moses did not live a life of splendor, eating and drinking joyfully. Throughout his time in the palace, he never once failed to worry about the Israelite people.

Among the Israelites in Egypt, only Moses maintained an unchanging loyalty toward heaven, regardless of whether his people knew it or not. Even while in the enemy's embrace, Moses resolved that he would not change, no matter what circumstances oppressed him or obstructed his heart toward heaven's will. Because Moses had this unchanging heart and sincerity toward heaven for 40 years, he was able to later unleash the power of love for his people.

You may see Moses as a hot-blooded person, but that is not the case. When he saw an Egyptian beating a Hebrew, his righteous anger did not arise from a moment of shock. Instead, when he witnessed that scene, the internal sorrow he had felt for 40 years, appealing to heaven with a heart full of anguish for his people, erupted. In other words, seeing the Israelites suffer injustice ignited an uncontrollable righteous anger within him, leading him to kill the Egyptian. Thus, love for the Israelite people and indignation toward Egypt were the internal causes of Moses' actions, and there was a providential meaning behind those actions.

Moses' act of killing the Egyptian out of indignation was done from the standpoint of worrying about and taking responsibility for the fate of the Israelite people, and compared to the sin of the Egyptian oppressing the Israelites, it was a minor offense. Therefore, God appointed Moses, who cared for the nation more than anyone else, as the leader of the nation. However, the Israelites misunderstood Moses and exposed his act of killing the Egyptian, forcing him to flee to the wilderness of Midian.

Living in the wilderness of Midian, Moses felt ashamed of the luxurious life he had led in the palace and forgot all the wealth and glory he had enjoyed in the free environment where the daughter of Pharaoh could grant him any request. Dressed as a shepherd, he became an anonymous shepherd, but while looking after his flock, he longed for the land of Canaan that had been promised to his ancestor Abraham.

Though he was now leading a flock, he had a heartfelt desire to one day lead his people into the land of Canaan, appealing to heaven with that longing. Whether he ate or fasted, slept or stayed awake, he devoted all his efforts to worry and pray for his people, just as Abraham prayed for the people of Sodom and Gomorrah without their knowledge.

When Moses looked upon the Israelites suffering under the oppression and misery of Egypt, he felt a sorrow that seemed to melt his bones and cried out to heaven, "O Lord! Look upon me and have mercy on this nation." Therefore, God appointed Moses, whose heart was filled with such earnest appeals, as the leader to lead 600,000 people out of Egypt, and even though he was living as an ordinary shepherd in the wilderness of Midian, he was made to inherit the integrity of the hidden roots passed down from his ancestors and was appointed as the representative of the nation. Thus, the Israelites were able to enter the land of Canaan, united with such a Moses.

When Moses received the promise granted from heaven and entered Egypt, he was filled with joy. However, Moses was not satisfied with just that joy. He had made a heartfelt appeal before heaven to dedicate his life to guiding his people into the land of Canaan, and while he was able to pave the way for the survival of the nation, he was not content with that joy alone; he felt a sense of mission and responsibility to faithfully fulfill a second responsibility.

From that point on, Moses did not act centered on himself, and he did not perform any task, whether small or great, without establishing a connection with God. 

Thus, Moses entered the oppressive palace of Pharaoh and performed more than ten signs and wonders before their gods, leading the Israelite people out into the perilous wilderness. Here, the Israelites had to become one with Moses. In other words, although they had escaped from the oppressive palace into a perilous wilderness, their hearts had to align with Moses' heart as they headed toward the blessings of Canaan. They could not have hearts that were different from Moses, who had rescued them from Pharaoh's palace. However, because they could not unite with Moses, they walked a path that contradicted heaven's principles and ultimately faced destruction. So, what was the reason for their destruction?

They did not understand the hidden sincerity that Moses had appealed with before heaven during the process of becoming the leader of the nation. Moreover, they did not recognize the hardships and efforts Moses had endured for them since the day he led them out of Egypt. As a result, they separated from Moses in the wilderness, and ultimately, they fell down in the wilderness.

This historical fact of the Israelites' disbelief in Moses is now reappearing among the saints of the end times.

Saints of the end times must act
Jesus Christ came to this earth and labored for humanity for over 30 years. After His death, for 2,000 years, He has sought humanity and worked through love and grace, yet people do not truly welcome such Jesus into their lives.

Just as the Israelites did not fully embrace God's will to lead them into the land of Canaan by disbelieving Moses, a fearful situation may also arise for the saints of the end times. When faced with the fact that they cannot unite with Moses, before rebuking the disbelieving nation, Moses appealed to heaven about his own shortcomings. He went up to Mount Sinai and fasted for 40 days, saying, "Father, why is it that this nation cannot enter the land that has been promised before their eyes? Whose responsibility is it? It is my responsibility. I have failed to take responsibility. Therefore, please use me as a sacrifice to prevent the destruction of this nation."

You must recognize that there was a period of hidden sincerity in Moses' life. If the Israelites had understood that Moses was fasting with a heart of anguish not for himself but for them, they would not have engaged in the foolishness of making a golden calf and worshiping it during Moses' 40-day fast. Furthermore, if they had sympathized with Moses, who was offered as a hidden sacrifice for the blessing of the nation, and had wept and appealed to heaven like Moses on Mount Sinai, they would not have strayed from God's embrace.

Just as Moses walked a lonely path representing the nation, Jesus also walked such a path. In other words, through the historical sacrifices of Abraham and the sacrificial path of Moses representing the nation, Jesus Christ was established at the center of the world. Just as Abraham represented his family to block Satan's accusations and Moses represented the nation to block Satan's accusations, Jesus had to stand alone to block all of Satan's accusations on behalf of all humanity and lay the groundwork for victorious redemption.

You must recognize that Jesus had this responsibility. Therefore, until He achieves victory globally and establishes an unchanging foundation, Jesus' mission must not end with just His own self. Thus, Jesus was more faithful than any central figure of faith who had been loyal before heaven throughout the 4,000 years of history, sacrificing His own self for the whole.

In this way, through over 30 years of His life, Jesus formed a central figure that represented the whole, something that no one in history had achieved. If He had not become such a central figure, you must understand that Jesus could not have become the vanguard bearing the responsibility of global providence.

Today, believing saints see Jesus as the one who bore the cross of one generation, but you must not believe in Jesus only as such. Before Jesus' death on the cross, there was the altar of effort built by Abraham and the sacrificial path that Moses had taken. Moreover, Jesus not only appealed to heaven, saying, "Please take upon Me the burdens of those suffering in pain and grant them the eternal ideals they seek," but He also did not live a single day comfortably to take responsibility for their suffering.

In this way, Jesus cared even for those in the enemy's embrace and lived from the standpoint of taking responsibility for the will of the whole rather than His own joy. Therefore, He was established as the victorious central being who triumphed over the world of Satan and became the Savior of all humanity.

So, what should we, the believing saints facing the end times, realize? We must reflect on the fact that we have not lived a life of shedding tears and worrying for the wicked. The more people there are who must face judgment at the end, the more we must pray for them. And we must not forget that there is Jesus, who worries for us and prays for us. If we forget and disbelieve such Jesus, we will not escape the judgment of the end times.

Saints of the end times must fulfill the mission of the root
If the people of Sodom and Gomorrah had accepted the warning of God's judgment given through Abraham and Lot, reflecting on their evil deeds and repenting, they could have avoided judgment. Historical facts teach us about future events, so today, at the end times...
must reflect on and repent for his past life. Therefore, we must be certain that just as Moses prayed for the unbelieving Jewish people when he ascended Mount Sinai, Jesus is also praying for us at this very moment on the spiritual Mount Sinai.

The heart of Jesus, who has been seated on the heavenly throne for two thousand years praying for humanity, surpasses the deep yearning of Moses, who prayed for the unbelieving Jewish people. Thus, you on the ground must recognize this and live according to Jesus' will. In the past, Abraham prayed to God to spare Sodom and Gomorrah if there were ten righteous people, but there were not even ten righteous people in Sodom and Gomorrah, and they faced God's judgment.

Therefore, just as Jesus has been praying for humanity from heaven since His crucifixion, and just as Moses prayed on Mount Sinai, we must empathize with that deep yearning and hold onto this era, worrying and praying in place of Jesus. Furthermore, you must not forget to be awake and seek where the one established by heaven, who can represent Jesus' global will and the prophetic figures of history, is located. If there is not even one person remaining as a root on this earth at the end of days, just as the Israelite people fell in the wilderness, we too will not be able to escape the fearful judgment when this world faces its global end.

So what should we do today? Because you are like hidden sparks, you must emerge through the spirit of Christ and become a being that responds to the hopes of your ancestors who have long awaited a central root. You must also be able to deeply feel the heart of Jesus Christ, who has labored for two thousand years, longing for the day of His return as if it were a single day. This is the issue. Therefore, you must now position yourselves in the relative position of historical central figures and examine and analyze yourselves. In other words, you must analyze whether you have placed yourselves in the position of Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, and whether you have become the embodiment of their hearts, your hearts, their wishes, your wishes, and their grievances, your grievances.

Now we must know how to stand before heaven with earnestness and build an altar of appeal. We must understand the heart of Abraham as he appealed to heaven for Sodom and Gomorrah. Abraham did not pray for Sodom and Gomorrah for his own children or for his nephew Lot. However, because Abraham forgot everything and built an altar of hidden sincerity, Lot, who was related to Abraham, was able to escape judgment.

Today, those who claim to believe pray, "Please fulfill my will." We should not pray such prayers. Rather, we should pray, "May Your will be done rather than my own." When heaven's will is fulfilled, my longed-for will will also be realized. Therefore, we should not pray, "Please fulfill my will." We must now, with all our sincerity, pray, "Abba Father, You have established me; You have called me; please fulfill Your will through me, Your humble servant."

Then what must you understand? The inheritance you have received is not just for your own generation but is the inheritance passed down from Abraham through Moses and Jesus.

You who live in this era must represent all the tribes since Moses and fulfill the will that heaven requires on behalf of the tribes that Jesus needed. Thus, even if this land is evil, even if this land is dark, even if this land is doomed, you must understand that you cannot help but become the hidden root established by heaven.

What heaven requires of us in this era
Heaven is asking us to fulfill the mission of religion based on personal faith at this time. What is that demand? It is whether we have fulfilled the responsibility that Abraham had. Next, it is whether you have labored with the same heartfelt concern that Moses had for the Israelite people when they were in distress, and whether you have poured out your heart and efforts for the thirty million Korean people who are in suffering, just like Moses did. And just as Jesus has labored to save all humanity from the beginning of creation until now, you will be asked whether you have worked for all humanity with the same heart and intention in place of Jesus.

Then, when asked if you have lived a life like that of Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, you should be able to respond, "Yes, do You not know us? The hidden root is not only within us but also within God." 

When you become such people, the purpose of establishing the faith through Abraham will bear fruit through you, the heartfelt pleas of Moses for his people will be resolved through you, and all the elements of sorrow that Jesus held for the world will be resolved through you.

If such a person exists on this earth, the heart that Abraham had for his generation, the heart that Moses had for his generation, and the heart that Jesus has had until now will be released. Therefore, if such a person exists, you must cherish them with all your sincerity. If there is no such person, you must understand that you should become that person, and if such a person exists, you should honor and serve them in place of Abraham, Moses, and Jesus. Thus, you should pray even more for your nation and act even more. Furthermore, you should become someone who builds an altar, even if you cannot be a sacrifice that can be offered to heaven.

For this reason, today you must call God "Father!" If you cannot truly feel the Father who has not been able to act as the Master throughout the historical process since the creation of heaven and earth, you will not be able to receive salvation in this generation. Therefore, you must, on behalf of all that, build an altar of prayer, just as Abraham prayed, just as Moses prayed, and just as Jesus prayed.

<Word> The title I wish to speak about today is "A New Covenant to Be Fulfilled." I will speak briefly with this title.

The meaning of the bread and wine that Jesus broke
For four thousand years, God has been carrying out the history of salvation through the providence of resurrection. Since the providence of resurrecting Jesus alone cannot complete the heavenly and earthly will, He established a new covenant and has been working to find the original garden promised by combining the heavenly and earthly wills.

Here, it is said that the cup that Jesus gave and the bread that Jesus broke are the new covenant. Since we have received the body and blood of Jesus after He came and went, we must understand that this represents the life of the whole to be fulfilled and simultaneously represents the truth of the whole.

What does receiving the blood and body of Jesus symbolize? It does not refer to the body and blood of Jesus as an individual. Broadly speaking, it signifies heaven and earth, and narrowly speaking, it signifies the center and the individual. Furthermore, the body symbolizes truth, and the blood symbolizes spirit.

All of this was unconditionally given to us by Jesus. You must understand that the body of Jesus that was given to us is not only a matter limited to itself but also encompasses the issues of all beings connected to it in heaven and earth.

What is the barrier between God and humanity? The heavenly will must be manifested on earth, and the overall situation on earth must be directed toward the heavenly will to move toward one purpose, but this has been blocked. Thus, Jesus, who was the protagonist of love, has been laboring until now to represent that one purpose that will appear in the victorious glory of heaven.

God labored for four thousand years to establish Jesus, symbolizing the ability to possess the entirety of heaven and the entirety of earth. Therefore, those who believe in Jesus can possess all of heaven and all of earth. However, what has been possessed must not be concluded as solely one's own but must be returned to heaven, as we have been entrusted with the overall will of providence.

Because Jesus established a new covenant, after His departure, there remained a condition for the spiritual world and the physical world to be connected through people, namely the apostles who followed Jesus. If Jesus had not died, heaven and earth would have been connected through Him, but because He died, Jesus became the condition for heaven, and the Holy Spirit became the condition for earth.

Who can stand in the middle position between heaven and earth and represent the will of Jesus and the will of the Holy Spirit? You must not forget that it is the apostles who have believed in the words of the new covenant on this earth until now, or us.

Where is the desire of Jesus? That desire is not in heaven. Where is the desire of humanity? It is also not on earth. The desire of Jesus must connect the earthly will, and the desires of the people on earth must connect the heavenly will. Therefore, you must become a sacrificial offering that represents heaven and earth as the body that represents the blood and body that Jesus personally broke for you.

If you do not do this, Jesus and the Holy Spirit will never be able to unite eternally. The Holy Spirit will continue to work on earth, and Jesus will continue to work in heaven.

What did Jesus say to His disciples? "You must eat my blood and my body." What does that mean? It contains Jesus' earnest heart, saying, "Even if I go, take all that has entered into the providence of the heavenly realm and fulfill my desires."

The blood received by the disciples from Jesus symbolizes the spiritual aspect of Jesus, and the body symbolizes the physical aspect, which represents the Holy Spirit. Thus, through the blood and body of Jesus, He wished to establish a central being that could move toward one purpose. And the blood and body of Jesus symbolized heaven and earth, respectively. Therefore, you must understand that there was a great hope and ambition of Jesus manifested in this.

Now, after you have become a holy body through the Holy Spirit, your heart must be connected to the body of Jesus. This symbolizes the process of restoration history. When Adam and Eve were created, a body was formed, and a soul was created. After forming the flesh, life was breathed into the nostrils to create Adam and Eve. Just as a person was created by combining the principles of two conditions, in the providence of restoration, Jesus...
The Holy Spirit, centered on you, has established a new covenant, and since then, the works of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, united in heaven and earth, have been connected until now. When considering this, you must understand how significant a responsibility lies upon us today. You must recognize that the heavens are influenced by the movements of insignificant apostles and our humble actions. You, who stand in place of the apostles! Upon receiving the body of Christ, the life force of Jesus, which can represent God, must manifest in you. The inspiration of the Holy Spirit, which can represent heaven, must also appear. When you unite as one in front of Jesus' will to restore all creation, when you turn left, heaven will turn left, and when you turn right, heaven will turn right. Heaven will move according to your movements.

If you do not establish the standard by which heaven can move through humanity, Jesus and the Holy Spirit will appeal to you. The universal mission left by Jesus will accuse you. When considering this today, you must feel that through us, who are nothing, Jesus wishes to fulfill a grand cosmic purpose that can influence heaven and earth. 

Jesus does not have the authority to decide without humanity. The Holy Spirit also does not have the authority to decide. Only we, as humans, possess the authority to make decisions.

The response to the blood and flesh received from Jesus
The history of the New Testament until now has been a history of "Please do this for us." It has been a history within the limits of hope. It has remained in a place that has not transcended any limits. We must go beyond the words of the New Testament. We must be able to receive the heavenly gifts beyond the history within those limits. We must advance with the entire value of Jesus, who sought to possess everything in heaven and earth with his own body, and be able to say, "Father, give me a new promise!" 

You must manifest the appeal of Jesus' blood and the appeal he made while tearing his flesh on the cross in your lives. The human responsibility that must be fulfilled for us to reach heaven has been promised through Jesus. However, it must not remain merely a promise. If my body possesses all the gifts of the whole and the hope of the new covenant, if my life has the ideal of that one life, and if I cannot establish a standard on earth that I can freely give, then you must understand that Jesus' resentment cannot be resolved.

We are currently in the process of fulfilling hope. We are in the process of looking towards a certain goal and achieving that hope. In this process, if you move, you must be able to conclude the promises of faith you have established. You must understand that a being that has transcended such limits is one that responds to the blood and flesh received at the last moment.

In this sense, what should I do? I must be able to represent Jesus in all directions, as well as the Holy Spirit in all directions, and God in all directions. If I cannot establish the day of conclusion through humanity, which is both the heavenly will and the earthly will, then you must understand that neither Jesus' will nor God's will can be realized. And when you think of such a will, you must realize how great the value of our insignificant selves is today.

What did Jesus require when he gave his disciples his blood and flesh? He took the cup, gave thanks, and said, "Divide this among yourselves." (Luke 22:17) You must not forget this. Since we have received the blood and flesh of Jesus, if we take responsibility for the heavenly issues in place of Jesus' mission, God's will will be fulfilled. This is the hope of heaven.

Today, we have the responsibility to build a relationship among ourselves based on the condition of having received Jesus' blood and flesh, and to seek the altar of victory. You must feel this responsibility deeply.

The Lord's will to love one another
The principles that come down from above do not change. Then, who will seek this unchanging principle of up and down, and the relationships that must be connected left and right? You must seek it. Jesus and the Holy Spirit have aimed in one direction with an unchanging center, regardless of historical changes and times. Just as Jesus and the Holy Spirit exchanged, we must establish such relationships among ourselves. If we cannot establish such relationships, you must understand that the altar where God can operate will not be realized on earth.

Do you understand the heart of Jesus, who shared his blood and flesh? It was an indescribably sorrowful heart. Even today, those who understand the will and seek to fulfill it endure trials that melt their bones in a pitiful and tragic place. Therefore, you must understand how Jesus feels when he sees those who do not feel this or do not know how to face such a will.

If you do not understand this historical situation, you cannot share the horizontal communion among yourselves. Therefore, today, when Jesus connects with God, and when Jesus connects with the Holy Spirit, we need to live in a way that we can share that love among ourselves, that is, to manifest the love of the Eucharist.

To connect individuals, to connect denominations, and to enter into one realm centered on heavenly love in any form, you must understand the Lord's request to love one another.

Today, among you, if there is someone who does not have a comrade who can give their whole self and receive that whole self in return, they must understand that they are a pitiful person. And the Holy Spirit before Jesus does not change even if people change, so He continues to exchange with them. Therefore, you must fight on behalf of the spiritual world based on the standard that can exchange like that.

Now the time has come for us to fulfill the last hope left by Jesus. How should you connect this one hope left and right? First, you must become someone who can serve on earth. You must become someone who fights and is martyred on earth. You must know how to serve the righteous on earth.

Today, you must remember what Jesus said. "Whoever serves others will be served." And "Whoever tries to exalt themselves will be humbled." This is the center of a life that we feel in a flat aspect today. Therefore, we must know how to serve anyone, become friends with everyone, and protect them.

To fulfill the new covenant
Now that the words of the new covenant have been promised, we must feel the inner heart that Jesus commanded. And we must be able to understand his heart, as well as his ideals and practical aspects. Thus, we must fulfill the will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. If such a will is not fulfilled in us, then at the end of days, the works of Jesus and the Holy Spirit will be gathered.

If the works of Jesus and the Holy Spirit are to be gathered, on that day of gathering, I must stand alone, knowing the hopes of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, and I must be a being who can walk the practical path that Jesus walked, possessing a new ideal on behalf of Jesus and the Holy Spirit.

We are those who have received the blood and flesh of Jesus' new promise. What mission remains for us? It is to fulfill the new covenant. To do this, even if my whole self does not have the cooperation of the Trinity at the end, I must be able to triumph over Satan. If so, what is the center that can triumph over Satan? It is the ability to act in ways that Satan cannot. We must be able to do what Satan cannot do.

The essence of Satan is pride. The essence of Satan is jealousy. The essence of Satan is self-interest. Therefore, the teachings of Jesus and the Holy Spirit are to be meek and humble, to sacrifice, and to become an offering. These are things that Satan cannot do. For Satan to be meek, he must repent of all sins before God and turn back. If Satan had no jealous heart, today this world would quickly return to God.

Therefore, you must equip yourselves with elements that oppose Satan within yourselves. Furthermore, you must not remain within that limit but must enter into the realm of the new promise beyond those limits. When you establish an unchanging center, as those who have received the blood and flesh of Jesus, you will be able to fulfill the meaning of the new promise.

If you cannot stand in a position where what God could not discuss with Jesus, and what Jesus could not share with the Holy Spirit can be discussed again because of you, that is, if you cannot stand as a central being representing all standards of heaven and earth, then you must understand that the meaning of Jesus' promise will not be fulfilled, and the meaning of the new promise that God desires will also not be fulfilled.

Today, even if we do not possess anything of the world, we must fully possess the body and heart of Jesus. We must be recognized as a central value representing heaven and earth from heaven. Thus, our recognized value must not remain within any limits. We must become a valued existence that no heavenly being can refuse to welcome.

The blood of Jesus and the flesh of Jesus do not only communicate on earth. They are not only applicable on earth. Just as the journey of faith is applicable in heaven, so too are they applicable in heaven. Therefore, if we have completely received the blood and flesh of Jesus, my wishes will be fulfilled in heaven and also on earth. And that fulfillment will represent Jesus' wishes in heaven and represent the Holy Spirit's wishes on earth.

Thus, we must advance to the point where we can take on the work that Jesus and the Holy Spirit did, allowing them to rest and enabling us to make a new promise with God. Only then will the new work of God, the overall providence of heaven, be conducted through you, establishing a standard of victory that you must keep in mind.
