<Word> The title I wish to think about with you all is, "Let us be those who welcome the Lord who came for all people." I will share a brief message on this topic.
God's creation ideal and the result of human fall
God, humanity, and all things were meant to be united forever centered around a single creation ideal, but because humanity, positioned between heaven and all things, made a mistake, all things became divided as they are, heaven as it is, and people as they are. Therefore, to regain the original world of creation, it was necessary to carry out the work of restoration, starting from all things, then humanity, and finally heaven. You must not be those who do not understand this situation of the Father.
We, born with the bloodline of the fall, as a fallen race, must first become those who feel God's sorrow deeply in our hearts and bodies.
Although we have all fallen, as long as there is a relationship with God who created us, and as long as there is a Father who is working hard to fulfill the providence, we must not think we stand in a meaningless position.
Even if you are evil, even if you are in a wicked place, you must first recognize that the traces of the tears of the Father's hard work are left on your bodies as you have gone through the historical process, and next, you must feel the traces of the Father's hard work and suffering that have been carried out to restore us.
Furthermore, we must understand that the original ideal of creation, the inner wish of God, exists for us at the end.
Then, we must realize that the sorrow of the intangible God is deeply embedded in our very beings, and that the signs of God's hard work, who is working for the restoration, remain in our bodies as a foundation of hope.
And we, who are on this earth, must become those who can bend our bodies and hearts to replace the sorrow of God with the sorrow we feel, as much as God has suffered with His painful heart and as much as He has worked hard, and as much as He has brought forth His original heart of goodness.
We must also understand that God is demanding that we have the heart of suffering that replaces God's hard work and that we can manifest the invisible suffering of God in a visible form. Furthermore, we must understand that God is seeking a religion of hope that can fulfill His wishes by discerning all historical religions.
Whether we are sitting or standing, whether we are active or inactive, at any moment of our lives or in a fleeting moment, God desires that true saints who can feel the touch in their hearts and bodies appear on this earth, and you gathered here today must move toward a place where you can feel this in your hearts.
The purpose of Jesus' coming and the disbelief of the Jewish people
Now, the creation ideal that the intangible Father had when He created humanity and all things was to enjoy joy and glory, to set humanity before all things, and to hope that all would be intoxicated by the ideal of goodness and boast of God's love while sharing joys and sorrows together. However, due to the fall of humanity, this ideal remained in His heart as a sorrow. The one who came to fulfill this mission was Jesus. And the one who came to tangibly resolve the core of God's inner resentment on behalf of humanity and all things, representing God's 4,000 years of hard work, was none other than Jesus Christ.
Then, where were those who should have welcomed Jesus, those who longed for Him, and those who could have shared eternal joys with Him?
The Jewish people at that time needed to understand that Jesus Christ was the one who could resolve the inner heart of God, who represented God's deep resentment, and who came to tangibly resolve God's resentment.
However, among the people of Israel, there was not a single person who could praise Him, recognizing that He was the one who could resolve the heart that God had grieved over for 4,000 years, the eternal hope that the Father was seeking.
The intangible sorrow of God must be resolved through tangible humanity. And Jesus was the one who could replace both God's sorrow and the sorrow of all people.
Yet, Jesus did not have a single day of joy throughout His life. Why? Because the tears of God's sorrow shed over 4,000 years were embedded in His heart, and even though all people should have united with Jesus to resolve God's sorrow, not a single person approached Jesus to empathize with His sorrow. There was not a single person who examined Jesus' life from beginning to end. Therefore, we must remember that such traces of resentment have been extended down to us today.
For the nation of Israel, who were hoping for the Messiah, it was unimaginable that the only begotten Son of heaven, born as the prince of heaven, would appear in such a sorrowful and shabby form.
That is why Jesus sought for a being who could welcome Him. He did not seek for someone centered around Himself, but rather sought for someone who could replace God's inner heart. Jesus sought a being who could participate in God's sorrow from birth, who could replace God's hard work from birth, and who could fulfill God's hope from birth, yet He found not a single such being, having been born in a stable and passing through over 30 years until He bore the cross.
Then, while Jesus who died on the cross can be welcomed by all, why was the living Jesus, who came with God's eternal love to convey that love to humanity, not welcomed by anyone? The responsibility lies with humanity. Jesus came to resolve God's sorrow and to remove the traces of God's hard work, and He came as the embodiment of God's hope to build the garden of hope, yet we failed to fulfill our responsibility to embrace His sorrow, carry His suffering within ourselves, and feel His hope in our hearts. This was the sin of our ancestors.
So what does Jesus demand of us today? The responsibility to resolve all of God's resentment through the body of Jesus has extended to us because our ancestors failed to fulfill it, and thus God's sorrow remains as Jesus' sorrow, God's hard work as Jesus' hard work, and God's hope as Jesus' hope, and furthermore, all of this has reached the Holy Spirit.
What Jesus demands of us today
Thus, the responsibility to resolve the sorrows of God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit, which have been extended through 2,000 years of history, lies with us today. You must feel this.
And there must appear a person who can resolve the 6,000 years of sorrow hidden in God's heart, a person who can replace 6,000 years of hard work. There must be someone among us who can manifest God's hope on this earth once again. We must find this person among us.
Now, when you stand before the amazing grace of the Father or the grace of Jesus Christ, you must not think that the day you step forward is the beginning. And when you stand before the Father, it is not just you standing there as an individual. You must realize that your belief is not just based on your own life but on the 6,000 years of history.
Even when you stand before the Father to repent of your sins, you must feel that this is not just a personal repentance but a repentance on behalf of 6,000 years. And when you have a heart of gratitude before the Lord's grace and love, you must not think that you are thanking Him alone in a single moment. You must become someone who can express gratitude on behalf of the entire providence of the Father, representing both the flat history and the three-dimensional history, and on behalf of a hopeful standard.
Thus, God desires that a person who can resolve His sorrow, a person who can take on His hard work, and a person who can fulfill His hope appears on this earth today.
Jesus, who came to tangibly fulfill the will of the Father, left this earth with the fate of having to return because He could not complete that work. Therefore, this Jesus will come again, seeking you, insignificant as you may be, with the sorrow of 6,000 years. He will come with not only the sorrow of 4,000 years but also the sorrow of 2,000 years added to it. Furthermore, He will come to you with the resentment of 2,000 years of hard work added to the sorrow.
Our responsibility regarding the returning Jesus
When Jesus, who comes with the hope of 6,000 years, appears before us, what is the responsibility of humanity? It is to tangibly take on the burdens of Jesus' heart, His sorrow, and His hard work.
Jesus came to the nation of Israel to resolve the sorrow of 4,000 years of hard work, yet the nation did not believe in Him and opposed Him, leading to His crucifixion. Thus, because there was not a single person among the people of Israel who could believe in and welcome Jesus as the one who came to resolve the sorrow of 4,000 years on behalf of the Father's hard work and the 4,000 years of history, Jesus had no choice but to die on the cross. Therefore, to complete this work, Jesus must return.
We, who are at the end of the age, which must conclude the 6,000 years of history, must stand alone before God and the Trinity and say, "Please let me take on Your sorrow as my sorrow. Please let me take on Your hard work as my hard work. Please let me take on Your hope as my hope." You must have the heart to prepare for the day of Jesus, knowing that although you are an individual, you can represent heaven and earth.
You must become the ones who are. You must become Christians of that world.

You, who must prepare for the second coming of Jesus, should once again reflect on the life of Jesus Christ, who came and went. You must become people who experience the circumstances of when Jesus was born, when Jesus lived, and when Jesus left as your own circumstances.

You should have the same sense of responsibility that Jesus felt when he realized that he had the duty to redeem all mankind with God's deep heart. You must have the heart that you personally lay in the manger where Jesus, who was born in a wicked land, lay alone.

Although Jesus is the prince of heaven, when he was born on this earth, how could he be laid in a stable? The sorrow of Jesus, overwhelmed with grief, is one thing, but the internal sorrow of God looking at that Jesus is beyond words.

You must feel that sorrow to the bone. Furthermore, you, who are in the end times, must feel the responsibility that I alone have taken on the mission that Jesus Christ bore.

And even though he came for all mankind, you must be able to think of the circumstances of Jesus, who was treated poorly and found himself in a pitiful position. If there had been a suitable being on this earth who could comfort Jesus in his sorrow, he would have had circumstances that made him want to hold onto that one person and pour out all his hopes.

However, the Jewish community, which God had chosen over 4,000 years and prepared for Jesus Christ, did not know Jesus. They had nothing to do with the Jesus who lay in the manger in the city of Bethlehem. This situation once again deepened God's sorrow. No one defended the Jesus who was born in a stable.

We must now become the ones who can take away and resolve God's grievances and the grievances of Jesus, who came and went on this earth. Only then can we remove the conditions for Satan's invasion from our bodies. And if we know that the Lord who will come again will appear on this earth in place of 6,000 years of history, we must not stand in the same position as the people of Israel.

Their faith was not centered on Jesus, nor on the Messiah, nor on God, but centered on themselves. The Messiah will surely come, yet knowing that, no one prepared to receive the Messiah.

When the wise men from the East proclaimed that they had come to worship Jesus lying in the manger in Bethlehem, the whole city of Jerusalem was in an uproar. It was the fortune-tellers from foreign lands who came to find Jesus. However, this uproar was not a joyful event. It was not a joyful event.

Preparation for the Lord who is coming again

You, who believe in heaven today, must not remain in the position of the Jewish community that made mistakes over 6,000 years of history. Now you must be able to prepare for the coming Messiah and not only relieve the sorrow of the first coming of Jesus but also give glory to Him. This responsibility lies with you.

Today, when you enter a spiritual stage, a place of discussion with the Father, many instructions will come down to you, telling you to do this or that.

When the Lord comes to this earth, there will be food, clothing, a place to stay, and activities. However, the Jewish people who longed for the Messiah did not know this and did not prepare to receive the Messiah. No one was waiting with even a single outfit prepared.

If there had been someone with such a desperate heart, when the three wise men came to Jerusalem and said so, the whole Jewish people would have followed the wise men to Bethlehem. However, on the way, there were only the three wise men.

This sorrowful mark left behind was the sin committed by our ancestors who claimed to follow God and uphold God's will. You must not stand in such a position today. You must be able to prepare to receive the coming Lord with your heart and body, inside and out.

Then, what must we, who are in the end times, and all Christians around the world, mobilize to do? If the Jewish people, who longed for the Messiah, had become a people who prepared a place for the Messiah to be born, they would not have laid Jesus in the manger. Likewise, Christians must become those who can prepare a place for the Messiah to be born.

Gifts for the Lord who is coming

You must not think of the fact that Jesus was wrapped in swaddling clothes and lying in a manger as something joyful. Jesus should have been laid in a position of glory, more than anyone on this earth, more than anyone in the 4,000 years of history. And as the Son of God, He should have been cherished and praised by all mankind. Moreover, He was the one who should be boasted of before Satan.

However, what must have been God's sorrow as He looked at the Jewish people who could not receive Jesus? You must understand this sorrow of God.

Therefore, you must now take on God's heart and, knowing the sorrowful heart of Jesus from 2,000 years ago, become someone who prepares gifts in secret. Heavenly gifts cannot be shown before Satan. They cannot be shown before people either. That is why the Bible says that the most precious gifts were not made known. Why? Because no one should know first. The one who should know must know first. If Satan knows first, it becomes a problem.

You must prepare gifts for the Lord who is coming, which are precious gifts that cannot be exchanged for anything on this earth.

When the Lord personally comes and acts, you must find a foundation of service in your own body so that the Lord does not feel difficulties either mentally or physically. This is because, above all else in this world, your body is the most precious thing.

This precious being, a reality that can replace the universe, must build a foundation of eternal peace when the beloved Son of the Father comes. And when the heart and body are united, when Jesus comes again, you must become the hands and feet of Jesus, live in place of Jesus, and comfortably receive Jesus. You must also become someone who can fight the battles that Jesus fought 2,000 years ago.

Jesus Christ fought for 2,000 years, and now you must have the heart to take full responsibility for that battle against Satan, and you must also have the heart to prepare the shield for that battle with your own body. And you must deeply empathize with the circumstances of Jesus at the time of his birth, and afterwards, you must empathize with the heart of Jesus while he lived on earth.

Tears and prayers of Jesus

If you truly seek the Father now, if you seek the embrace of Jesus' love, you will shed tears.

God has been sorrowful for 4,000 years but could not express that sorrow, while Jesus lived with tears. Although it is mentioned only in a few places in the Bible, the hidden truth of Jesus shedding tears is countless.

When God looked at the Jewish people whom He has loved through providential history for thousands of years, there was never a moment when He did not shed tears. Every time Jesus prayed before God, He shed tears. Whenever He faced difficult and lonely situations, Jesus grieved in a way that only the Father could understand. However, Jesus could not speak of this sorrow to His disciples. You must understand this situation of Jesus.

Jesus went up to the Mount of Olives and prayed all night, and this was not just a one-time occurrence. He did not only pray in the Garden of Gethsemane.

While walking a difficult path, there was no place to express His sorrow except for heaven. Yet, He did not intend to entrust that sorrow to heaven. Rather, He asked to bear that sorrow Himself.

"Father! I will take on the sorrow that makes You grieve. Father! Please find comfort in me! I will bear Your sorrow, so do not grieve." This was the kind of appeal He made. And He prayed, "I will take responsibility for the labor of 4,000 years, so Father, do not worry. I am here, so do not worry that Your hope is lost."

From the time He became aware, Jesus had sorrow. He experienced sorrow from the moment He grew up because the people of the world did not receive Him.

Jesus grew up as a stepson in Joseph's household. So, although the whole village spoke much about Jesus, He lived a life of silence. He grew up as an ordinary child while harboring the unexpressed, great, and amazing will of heaven. You must not think that the life He lived as a carpenter for 30 years was a good life. Jesus, who should have stood in a more noble position than anyone in the nation of Israel, revealing the joy and glory of the Father, lived to support Joseph's life by carrying a plane and a chisel. What kind of statement is this?

Today, if there are sons and daughters who wish to uphold God's will and want to relieve God's grievances, they must learn to walk by following the example of Jesus.

If you want to know the life of Jesus, you must resonate with the heart of Jesus, who replaced the amazing gifts, empathize with that heart, and enter into that difficult position. Then you will realize that Jesus' sorrow transcends time and daily life, and that Jesus' life was a life where He could never feel peace at any moment.

However, Jesus, who came for the earth, grieved so that He would not turn the sorrows of the earth to heaven. Today, those who believe in Jesus often try to pass their own crosses and sorrows to heaven. We do not believe in Jesus for that reason. However, the sorrow of heaven is the sorrow caused by me, and I will bear that sorrow. "God, do not worry," is the mindset of someone who has experienced a part of Jesus' belief and life.

Are you my friend?

Now, if the footprints of Jesus' sorrow, who lived for over 30 years with tears, remain, you have the responsibility to relieve them.

Jesus lived in sorrow for over 30 years and ultimately bore the cross and passed away, but at the final moment, He cried out, "Abba, Father, why have You forsaken me?" yet was filled with a painful heart to fulfill His purpose.

Then, if today you look at the world with the heart that I am a friend of Jesus, you will not be able to look at this world without tears. Jesus shed tears every time He moved His feet, every time He moved His body. There was never a moment when He did not shed tears. Similarly, among the believers today, if there is someone who lives each day with a heart of repentance before heaven, that person will become a friend of Jesus.

In churches and families, if there are people who can shed tears for one another, knowing the heart of Jesus and wanting to comfort God, there will surely be infinite life and love present, even without demanding it from God. You must understand that God is seeking Christians who can connect with His circumstances, emotions, and content.

If the Lord were to come to this earth today, He would ask, "Are you truly my friend who has endured over 30 years of suffering?" He would also ask, "To what extent have you embraced God's painful heart, and how many days have you lived with the world's sorrows?"

You must understand that because humanity did not receive Jesus, they handed Him over to Satan as a condition. And you must overcome this condition.

Why do we live today? Before this body dies, before this dust enters my eyes, we must become people who can hold onto the life of Jesus and cry out, and become true people who can raise up what was trampled in Jesus' life. Therefore, you must fulfill this responsibility while you are alive.

That is why today, I am not just a simple "me." You must not think of yourself as just the age you have lived so far. Each of you must feel that you carry a cosmic mission to bear the fruits of God's restoration providence from Adam and Eve to Jesus and the 2,000 years since Jesus.

Therefore, just as Jesus stood boldly before His enemies, you must also be bold even if you face the suffering of the cross. Even if you shed tears, do not shed them for yourself; if you cry, do not cry for yourself.

If you are to cry, cry for Jesus. Then how joyful will Jesus, who thinks of you and cares for you, be? And God will understand your circumstances. Even if you shed tears, you must become someone who sheds tears with that heart. Those who shed tears for themselves are not needed. Only those who shed tears and repent for Jesus and God's love will become the sons and daughters of God.

When you face the suffering of the cross, if you truly feel the love of the Father and feel that you are within the realm of the Father's love, you may find it hard to pray. I have felt that way. Even when a burden as heavy as a thousand tons was placed on my shoulders, I did not pray, "Father, lighten this burden for me." 

Such prayers should not be made.

The loving Father knows me in such a position. If I were to pray, "Father, I am carrying such a burden," to the Father, who is already in a sorrowful position, I would only bring a second sorrow to the heart of the suffering Father.

You must understand even these things and approach God and Jesus. Even if there are only a few people with such a heart among thirty million people, they can prevent the sorrows of this nation. We must never appear to be crying because of our own sorrows.

Jesus, who was anxious to comfort the Father

Jesus came to this earth with a cosmic mission but suffered throughout His life. However, He did not pray for His own sorrow; rather, He was anxious to comfort the Father's heart and alleviate His concerns. While looking at the earth, He was pained to tolerate the ignorance of humanity. However, Jesus' life did not end merely as a life of tears for over 30 years. He stepped forward to take on God's labor, living with the heart to glorify the Father's will, whether He lived or died.
Jesus lived for the purpose without caring whether God recognized Him or not, whether people on earth acknowledged Him or not, and regardless of time and place. Although Jesus came to completely fulfill His purpose, He did not despair or feel troubled when He was crucified. Even when He went to the place of death, Jesus did not justify Himself. As you know, He did not make excuses as He went through Pilate's court, up to the summit of Golgotha, and was nailed to the cross. He was the protagonist without excuses. Jesus felt it was His responsibility that people opposed Him like that. We, who believe in Jesus Christ, must become friends of Jesus, who lived as the incarnate Jesus and as the resurrected Jesus.

What did Jesus become friends with? He did not become friends with life but became friends with death. Many people have walked the path of death throughout history, but only Jesus became a friend of death on behalf of all humanity and died on behalf of all. Therefore, Christianity is a religion of death and sacrifice, and the truth of Christianity is the truth that overcomes death. Jesus's activities were about destroying His own body. Yet, we must recognize that His path was one of love without resentment.

Because Jesus was a friend of death, even when death was imminent, He did not care about it. You must understand that He lived a life that could die for His enemies. In the end, even God said He did not know the Jesus who was crucified. At that time, Jesus cried out, "Abba, Father, why have You forsaken me?" This was not a cry of despair that all hope seemed lost, but a cry of concern that He could not fulfill the Father's will completely due to His death. Because Jesus had fulfilled His responsibilities, He did not care whether the Father sent Him to heaven or hell. Jesus, who was in a position to be a friend of death, sought to be satisfied with dying and to fulfill His mission through death.

Jesus came with cosmic love, but no one recognized it. Although He brought such an amazing gift, once He embarked on the path to become a friend of death, He had no lingering attachments. He came to fulfill the hope of heaven, yet even when heaven did not respond to that hope, He did not argue or complain.

When we seek God, there is a final peak. Even if you put forth your utmost sincerity, there may come a time when heaven says it does not know you. When heaven says it does not know, it is because a global mission is set before us. Therefore, Jesus also had to bear a global mission, which is why He faced such circumstances. Likewise, you will encounter such situations. Even if you devote yourself and your life to the Father, there will be times when heaven says it does not know.

However, you must be able to say that whether you live or die, it is the Father's will. If you have hope, you must have the hope of fulfilling the Father's will alone. You must become a person who can say that not eating or not wearing something is a joyful matter.

The final peak on the path to seeking God
Today, you must not become a person who believes in Jesus to go to heaven. Those who believe in Jesus to die will go to heaven. If you believe in Jesus not to live well but to die well, that will be a precious faith. Where did the twelve apostles, who hoped to live well, go when Jesus died?

You must believe not for your life to live well, but to sacrifice your life well, that is, to die well. To do this, we must resemble the life of Jesus. We have the responsibility to uphold the life of Jesus in history. We have the responsibility to carry His life. Only by having the life of Jesus can we have the love of Jesus. We can only receive the love of Jesus by welcoming Him. You must also have the character of faith that can emulate the hard work Jesus has done for two thousand years.

Moreover, since God's providence has been extended for six thousand years, you must be able to welcome the one who will take responsibility for that six thousand years of providence. You must have the time to invite and welcome the Father or the Lord when He appears to you. That time should not be just one or two hours but should be eternal.

So how can you qualify to welcome the Lord? Above all, you must be able to take responsibility for the sorrow of God's six thousand years and comfort Him. You must be able to go before the Lord who has labored and say, "I will do this and that. I will welcome You in this way. I have prepared this and that." You must be a saint who can say, "Lord, come! Lord, reveal Yourself!" Such a saint cannot fail.

This great mission lies before us. However, many people do not know this. They do not realize that the internal heart of Jesus and His internal hope revolve around each one of us today. What will happen to such people? Those who do not know will perish. The time will come when they will strike their own chests.

To welcome the coming Lord
You must welcome Him with your heart, with your body, with society, with the world, and with heaven and earth; this is the responsibility of the sons. Yet today, you cannot even welcome Jesus with your heart. You must realize that you have not even started to welcome Jesus.

Welcoming Him with your heart, with your body, with society, with the nation, with the world, and with heaven and earth should bring glory not only to you as individuals but also to your families, societies, nations, and the entire created world. You may not have imagined that such a universal mission exists for you.

Therefore, you, who have gathered with this mission, must not be petty. You must not become cowardly or foolish. Even when facing countless enemies, you must stand tall. You have the responsibility to welcome Jesus, who comes with cosmic glory and cosmic love. You must step forward with your heart and substance into the cosmic position.

However, Christians who are satisfied with just being diligent for themselves or their families are not needed. Christians who are satisfied with just one church are not needed. Even if thirty million people are all Christians, we need representative Christians who can stand on behalf of the nation. Even if all two billion people in the world believe in Jesus, we need representative Christians who can stand on behalf of those two billion people.

We must qualify to govern all the angels in the spiritual world, and we must be able to say boldly that we have done such a valuable work before them. To do this, Jesus Christ came.

Jesus, who came to fulfill such a great mission, is the Jesus we must earnestly welcome. Yet how have we lived as we look toward Him? We have no face to show. Even if we shed tears for six thousand years, it is not enough. Even if we beat our chests and weep for six thousand years, it will not be enough. We must not become shameless people in such a position.

Even if you must die immediately, even if you must fall and be trampled, you must not change the integrity and loyalty you possess. You must be able to stand boldly before all creation and establish the dignity of the children of heaven.

Children of integrity and loyalty
You stand on a difficult path. No, you stand on a path of fate from which you cannot turn back. On this path of fate, you must carry your beliefs and inner loyalty throughout your life.

You must weep. 
Even if I welcome the Lord, I must welcome the global Lord, the cosmic Lord, the Lord who transcends six thousand years of history and embodies the eternal ideal world. I must welcome such a Lord, yet I have only been satisfied with welcoming the Lord of my family or the Lord of my nation.

You must repent and weep for this.

Do you feel the responsibility and mission for this era? Have you ever thought that you must fulfill the ideals that all humanity has hoped for from the beginning of creation until the end when the ideals are completed? Have you felt such a cosmic sense of mission?

Moreover, you must have the mindset that you are a person who can fulfill such a mission and still have something left. When you pray from that standpoint, you will not need many prayers. If there is someone in that position, just one word, "Father!" will resonate completely. There is no need for explanation. There is no need for logic.

Before speaking, we must qualify to step forward without hesitation due to the intuitive shock of the heart. We have stepped forward with such treasures. Now that you have started, are you not bound by any conditions? Are you not stopping at some point along the way? In your life journey, how far have you come? You must start from the individual and run through family, society, nation, and world, all the way to heaven and earth. You must recognize that there is such a universal mission. Only then can you meet the Lord.

Jesus Christ is looking for a true person who can welcome Him, to shed all the sighs of six thousand years, to hold onto Him and shed tears of gratitude, saying, "Father, the being You wished to find is here. Father! Rejoice!" On that day, a glorious response from heaven saying, "Yes!" must come forth before humanity.

You, who fight with that day as your standard, must fight today and fight tomorrow, becoming someone who can dedicate your entire life. Thus, you must become a pioneer in the path of eternal life, a vanguard, and be adorned as a cosmic bride who can welcome the cosmic Lord.

You must remember that you cannot stop fighting until you receive the glory of victory, the love of the Father, and eternal life, becoming a bride representing all creation and the entire universe, and until you can eternally share joy and sorrow with the Father.

Chosen ones for the restoration of the kingdom of heaven
John 15:1-22
<Prayer (I)> Now we have reached the last Sunday of this year. Father, when have we ever thought of Your heart and worried about it? When have we fought for Your work? When have we truly loved You?

Father, please forgive us for not being able to fulfill the responsibilities You entrusted to us with a heart of concern throughout this year. There have been many commands and orders You have given us while placing us in this insignificant position, yet we have not fulfilled that mission. Please allow this body to accomplish the great purpose You require.

Please forgive the people on earth who do not know the times and seasons and cannot move toward the standard of fulfilling the desires of heaven. Even though we have come through the path of struggle, we cannot help but feel ashamed when we see that the fruits of victory have not appeared before You.

To Your sons and daughters gathered here, please reassign all the responsibilities You entrusted to us in the past, so that we may run for Your will. Grant us the discerning hearts to know when we can receive Your love, both internally and externally.

Father, the mission You have entrusted to us is not just to find ourselves today, but to find the nation, the world, and to resolve the grievances of heaven. We feel humbled before You, as we must follow Your commands.

Father, please raise us, who are weak and lacking, before You, and allow Your mercy and grace to overflow beyond this place and into the world of Satan. We earnestly desire this.

Father, have mercy on this nation. Have compassion on the countless churches gathered on behalf of this nation. Allow them to know the great purpose and providence You have.

So that each church may uphold Your will, and each nation may uphold Your will, please allow this nation to fulfill Your will, so that all two billion people in this world may fulfill Your desires and that the day may come when all humanity can sing of that glory.

On this day, we present all our shortcomings and gather before Your knees, believing in Your merciful love. Please protect us with Your love of mercy, embrace us with the gifts of glory, and uplift us with new courage and new strength. Father, we earnestly desire this.

Now, in this hour, may heaven and earth rejoice with You, and may Your good love dwell in this place, allowing us to return the glory that is bound in the oneness between You and us, and to receive love from You.

There are sons and daughters kneeling alone in the regions, building altars before You. If we have entrusted the entire mission of the end times to them, please allow them to represent Your will and manifest only Your will wherever they are. We earnestly ask for this.

On this day, may the glory of joy be upon the heads of all, and we pray in the name of our beloved Lord. Amen.
<Prayer (II)> Father! We thank You for finding and raising us, allowing us to fight until this time. Today, we have a mission to fight for a day of Your glory with all our body and heart, so please allow us not to grow weary.

Father, as we follow Your command to go, even on the difficult path where we cannot turn back, we have felt so much that You are with us, even on the path of death. We cannot help but thank You for leading us and enduring so much for us.

Father! It has been a long time since the promised day and the day of permission have passed, and we feel ashamed before the purpose You have granted. Now, Your sons and daughters gathered here, if we cannot repay Your glory on this day, please allow us to repay it with tears.
Father! According to the command to endure and bear, please allow the wishes of our ancestors who have appealed for this nation to be fulfilled at this end time. We earnestly hope and wish that You will quickly reveal Your will before all humanity and give us Your command. 

Father, among the sons and daughters gathered on behalf of the nation, are there any children who do not realize Your great will? Please allow us to understand the heart of the Father that pierces our bones and flesh.

We know that the path we must take is long and treacherous. No matter what barriers may arise before us at any given day or hour, please grant us the strength to break through, and do not allow us to become those who blame before our enemies. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

Father! Please allow the sons and daughters gathered here today to settle all matters and resolve everything that has been entangled for 6,000 years. While we resolve our individual shortcomings, please allow us to also resolve the shortcomings of this nation in this one place. Thus, please allow us to settle all the shame that has existed throughout the 6,000 years of human history. By doing so, may this time become a day when we can establish a condition of victory before Satan and overcome. Father, we earnestly hope for this.

Father, please allow us to be like children who know nothing. Let us be those who only know how to obey when led, and who only know how to submit when guided. Please allow us not to have any of our own opinions or concepts remaining, and let us become a good group resembling the pure heart of a child, so that whether we live or die, we may keep this one path, and even if it is a path of blood and flesh being torn apart, please allow us to run forward. We earnestly hope and wish for this.

There are lonely family members widely spread in the regions, prepared to fight and keep Your will, even at the cost of their lives, so please do not let them become weary. At this time, please grant them courage and the impulse of righteousness, so that they may welcome a day of joy and glory under a new determination and new resolution. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

At this time, please tolerate our shortcomings. We have nothing to boast of and nothing to carry. We only have a desperate heart that wants to be embraced in the arms of Your love like a little child, so Father, please manifest Yourself at this time and discern each heart, and bless us according to the measure You have created. We earnestly hope and wish for this.

Among the sons and daughters gathered here today, please do not allow any to be led away by Satan, and let this one hour be a time of determination to raise the flag of joy and victory, so that we may forever give glory to You, Father, with a shout of Hosanna. We earnestly request this, and I pray all these things in Your name. Amen.

<Prayer (III)> Father! We have learned through the Word that heaven and earth are one body. When we think that heaven is the subject and we are the chosen people for the restoration of the heavenly kingdom, we realize that we cannot live even for a single day or a single moment without receiving the essence of heaven's love and life. Yet today, we have not been able to live receiving the essence of love that comes from the eternal God as a single leaf and branch of heaven. Please forgive us.

Father! Now that the end time has come and the day of judgment is imminent, please allow us to be grafted into Your love centered on Jesus Christ, who is the perfect root. We know that You are our Father, who longs to harvest the fruits of love that are bound together through Your eternal love and the love of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. However, we are so inadequate, imperfect, and immature that we fear becoming obstacles to Your harvest.

Now we entrust ourselves to You, Father! Please nurture and care for us. Allow us to be refined through trials and tribulations, so that we may be completed as a mature fruit. Through the touch of Your eternal love, let us become the fruit that establishes the eternal kingdom of heaven and become harvesters who can gather.

Father! This was not something that was first foretold today, but it is something that was already foretold long ago in the Old Testament and during the time of Jesus 2,000 years ago. Knowing this, we must become the harvest that can be gathered before heaven today, and we must become the fruit that can bring rest to heaven. However, when we examine ourselves, there may still be those who do not feel completeness. If that is the case, please allow us to repent before You and become children of repentance who can take the place of Jesus Christ's sorrow, as we lament our inadequacies. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

Father, as we gather on this day, please fully govern their hearts and let them be governed as the center of Your operation. Do not allow any evil concepts or claims that are unworthy before Your will to be tolerated.

Let those gathered here be completely sanctified children by adding sanctification upon sanctification, and let this one hour be a time when only You can operate and only You can intervene. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

Now, please allow us to understand that You are urging the establishment of the day of Christ through us, and let us recognize that this is the time when You wish to manifest the love of Christ through us. Also, let us understand that You are longing for us to embrace the tribulations of Christ in this 20th century. Father, please guide our steps toward the heavenly nature so that we do not center ourselves, and do not allow us to remain in a place of self-centered prayer.

Please allow us to break free from all elements that can be invaded by evil. No matter how treacherous the path may be to fulfill Your will, even if it is a path where we may fall and despair, please hold us and help us endure. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

We know that we are not of the earth, and therefore cannot receive the glory of the earth. As You foretold through Jesus Christ, after passing through 2,000 years of history, there are heavenly people, children of heaven, who possess true love and true principles of the Father. We know that they have not been welcomed on earth in any century or era.

Father! Today, as we stand in the place of Jesus, please allow us to endure when the altar that will fulfill what Jesus could not accomplish on earth faces persecution. Even when we live for heaven and face humiliation, hardship, and sorrow from humanity on this earth, please allow us to overcome and remain steadfast.

Today, after 6,000 years, Jesus is calling us, longing for the day of harvest. Please gather the historical sorrows and the traces of the blood and tears of the cross through us, and guide us to become shields of victory. Let us know that the embodiment of hope, Jesus, is still hoping that we will become those who can govern Satan.

Thus, we must bear the joyful will of the Father in our hearts and fight on behalf of heaven today. If this mission does not end in our lifetime, please allow us to be sons and daughters who resolve to subdue the enemy Satan through our descendants. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

As we approach the new year, we must deeply prepare ourselves for the path of battle that risks life and death. No matter what enemies oppose us, may all sons and daughters be able to uphold their loyalty here. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Thus, please allow us to clearly reveal ourselves as the sons and daughters who represent You before all creation and to be Your sons and daughters who can stand in place of heaven and earth. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

On this day, please manifest the words You have allowed, soften the hearts, and let spirit move spirit, so that we may be reshaped before the touch of Your powerful hand. We earnestly request this, praying all these words in Your name. Amen.

<Word> The title I wish to think about with you is "The Chosen People for the Restoration of the Heavenly Kingdom." I will briefly speak on this title.

The End Time of the Providential History Where One Must Confirm Their Position

Today, we have reached the last Sunday of this year. If we do not fulfill the mission entrusted to us this year, we must fulfill it next year, and if we do not take responsibility for today, we must surely do so tomorrow. You all know this well through the Principle of Restoration.

The history since creation has passed through days, years, and long periods, with times and seasons changing, and 6,000 years have elapsed. However, now a great judgment is unfolding globally on this earth, and the providence of restoration that God must complete must be realized through you today, through the 2.4 billion humanity.

Now, facing the end of the 6,000 years of providential history, we who have joined to cooperate in the cosmic restoration history must clearly find our own position where we stand.

Therefore, each of you must reach the standard of the ideal of the final restoration that transcends the 6,000 years of history, and the center of creation, Adam and Eve. Furthermore, your families, society, and all of humanity must all surpass that standard. Until that standard is surpassed, God's providence will not conclude on this earth.

Thus, the tremendous and fearful labor of the restoration providence, the transgressions committed by our ancestors, and the parts they could not bear must be taken responsibility for and fulfilled by us, their descendants today. You must feel that you have this cosmic mission at this time.

Because Adam and Eve fell, the ideal of the heavenly kingdom was fundamentally destroyed, and the ideal of the heavenly kingdom that was to be completed through humanity fell completely from heaven. And still, we have not found the heavenly kingdom, nor the people to establish it, nor the families to form the people, nor the couples and children, and siblings to form the families.

The Restoration of the Heavenly Kingdom and the Right Life of Humanity

Therefore, the central purpose that God requires is the restoration of the heavenly kingdom. And the movement to restore the heavenly kingdom must be done as a gathering of the harvest. We must restore from the heavenly people to the children of heaven, the brothers of heaven, the couples of heaven, and the families of heaven to establish the heavenly kingdom. This mission remains for us.

The land we live in today, this world we live in today, is not the land of the heavenly kingdom, nor is it the world of the heavenly kingdom. It is a world centered on Satan, opposed to the heavenly kingdom. However, a historical turning point where the world of evil is restored to the good heavenly kingdom will surely appear at the end of history.

Today, the 2.4 billion humanity is overcoming the peaks of restoration according to God's providence, moving from individual restoration to family restoration, societal restoration, national restoration, and world restoration.

The central purpose of the gospel that Jesus Christ preached when He came to this earth was also the restoration of the heavenly kingdom. This standard of restoration means not only the restoration of your individual selves but also the restoration of families, societies, nations, and the world, ultimately to the cosmos. Therefore, from the day you believed in Jesus, you have been on the path of struggle for restoration.

The lives of people in the world today are not lives lived for the world. They say they live for the nation, but they do not truly live for the nation. They say they live for the family, but they do not truly live for the family. They also say they live for themselves, but they are not truly in a position to live for themselves.

Today, all humans in the world of evil must live for the world, yet they are not able to do so. Humans who should live for the nation, the people, the tribe, the family, and themselves have fundamentally lost that position.

Today, even though humans are centered on themselves, they cannot live centered on their hearts. When looking at myself, I have fallen to a degree where I cannot live centered on my heart, even though I should be living centered on my heart. I have become one who lives centered on the flesh. I have become one who lives only for physical satisfaction centered on myself.

In order to restore fallen humanity, God has been working to establish the body to subdue the heart, to establish the individual to subdue the family, to establish the family to subdue the nation, to establish the nation to subdue the world.

Therefore, in any society, individualistic people have stood in opposition to the revolutionary path of coming to believe in Jesus Christ. Those who have come centered on the family have also stood in opposition.

God works according to the progress of history, that is, according to the progression of the individual era, family era, national era, and the era of the state. In that progression, there have been difficult hurdles that humans could not follow.

The Center We Must Aim For and the Order of Restoration

Today, in this time when the 6,000 years of history is concluding, the ideology of Jesus Christ has been established as the ideology of restoration for the entire world on this earth. In other words, the ideology centered on Christianity is now appearing as the central ideology of the world. However, here, we are facing a counterattack from the enemy's ideology, and these two paths are in conflict.

Then, what standard should we aim for today? Through the hope of Jesus Christ, who established the ideology of the restoration of the heavenly kingdom, the ideal garden we must go toward is not just this world. The standard of restoration that God seeks is not just this earth. It is the ideology of the garden where heaven and earth unite as one, not two. Thus, God has been working to find a day of glory where we can harmonize and sing centered on heaven.

What we must understand in this time is that we must indemnify and restore all the sins of our lives.

Even when you come to believe in Jesus, a personal struggle will unfold. There will be a struggle between the body and the heart. Those who become casualties in that struggle cannot become citizens of the heavenly kingdom. When the evil movements centered on the flesh try to subdue the heart, if they cannot subdue it and achieve victory, they cannot become citizens of the heavenly kingdom.

Today, we have a mission to restore from the world to the nation, from the nation to the people, from the people to the family, from the family to the couple, and from the couple to the children and siblings. Because there is a principled standard of God's heavenly kingdom, we must first restore ourselves.
Heaven is in your heart. While you must complete the universal heaven, you must first complete your personal heaven. What this means is that you must establish a relative standard of body and mind to become a being that can stand before the Heavenly Parent.

Therefore, now you can be absorbed and harmonized in any field beyond the entirety of heaven, and to put it in terms of a tree, Jesus is the vine, and we are the branches of the vine, and we must take on the shape of a branch in any aspect. Thus, as branches, you going out through the trunk is what constitutes the return to heaven.

The stage of returning as citizens of heaven
The first stage you must seek is the stage of becoming citizens of heaven. The destiny to enter the stage of citizens of heaven is laid before you. You must renew your historical consciousness. Your existence should not be for yourself, but you must have the idea of being for your fellow citizens of the heavenly kingdom. Furthermore, you should have the idea of wanting to strive for the brothers of heaven, the couples of heaven, and the parents of heaven. This is not a partial idea but a universal idea. You must possess such a universal idea.

Moreover, if you live in society today, you must have the consciousness of that society, and if you live in a nation, you must have a national consciousness. If you belong to one nation, you must be able to love the people of that nation. Today, we must become people who can assert our will before God, who is working to build heaven. We must be able to love the citizens of heaven. We must recognize that we exist for the purpose of building heaven and for the world return, which is the will of the Father.

As mere believers in Jesus, we should not blindly serve Jesus, but we must become people who can believe in Jesus by harmonizing internally and externally with the fortunes of heaven and earth. God is establishing the ideology of the return to heaven centered on universal providence. We must become sons and daughters, and a people who can stand there. And we must be able to love our fellow citizens of heaven.

If there are believers among the many people around you, you must become someone who can regard them as brothers and fellow citizens. You must also encourage everyone to do the same. In light of this, your responsibility is immeasurably great.

So what does God require of us today, at the end times? It is for the believing saints to mobilize and build the garden of heaven. Thus, each individual must unite, and each nation must unite to form the citizens of heaven. You must understand this.

Looking longitudinally at 6,000 years of history, in the Old Testament era, the heavenly people were gathered, and in the New Testament era, the children of heaven were gathered. History has flowed like this, like a fisherman’s net.

Today, there are people in the world who are trying to build heaven centered on the ideology of the citizens of heaven. There are also those who seek to build heaven based on the ideology of heavenly children, heavenly brothers, and heavenly couples.

Standards of heavenly law and standards of heavenly life
Now you must learn to keep the laws of heaven in your daily life. To fulfill what heaven requires for the construction of heaven, you must know how to keep the laws of heaven. At the same time, you must know how to live a heavenly life. And while knowing how to live a heavenly life, you must become one in the love of heaven.

Then, what should we center on to keep the laws of heaven, as God has been working to restore heaven? We must keep the laws of heaven centered on the biblical words delivered to us through Jesus. Since the word is the law of heaven, we must live centered on the word. Here lies your path. In particular, you must live keeping the laws of heaven centered on the principle words that testify to internal truths through the biblical words.

So how should life be lived? You must live a life that substitutes for Jesus' thirty years of life. Your life today, in the end times, must be a life that testifies to Jesus Christ. Therefore, you must be able to show your life before all people. You must live a life like that which Jesus showed us.

You must live a life for heaven by following the life of Jesus, who kept the laws centered on God's word. Therefore, you must now live a life that substitutes for Jesus' life centered on the laws of heaven. Your hope and ideals must be God's love. Thus, to connect with God's love, you must establish conditions of harmony. This is what God is demanding from all Christians in the world today.

The sap of one branch flows into another branch. It circulates through any leaf or branch. In the same way, you must become someone who can harmonize with and support each other. Such a person will be able to possess the remaining love of God as an ideal.

Abandon the concept centered on oneself
Therefore, we Christians must abandon the concept centered on our individual selves and adopt a new concept that my existence represents the world and the universe.

Thus, when looking at our family members, we must understand that today’s person is not just that person. You must feel that they represent 6,000 years of history, represent eternal providence, and represent 2.4 billion humanity in a flat sense. Regardless of who it is, there is the promise of universal God's love in them. Therefore, you must become a collaborator before such a person. Because you have such a mission, you must be able to see the will of God's providence correctly and become a people who represent that will.

This applies to your personal life and family life as well. Your own children, your own parents, and your spouse do not exist for you. Your children are not your children for your sake, nor are your siblings for your sake, nor your parents. They exist for the sake of the nation, for the world, and for the Heavenly Parent.

We must know this and treat our children, siblings, and parents from that perspective. If you recognize and feel this in your life, you will not be able to speak of any person lightly.

We must not forget that there is a universal will of God in our individual selves. My existence is not for myself but exists for the world and for heaven and earth, representing the mission of return. Knowing this, all of you must live in unity.

Today, those of you who have come out on a so-called extraordinary path must now depart from a self-centered life. You must abandon the concept centered on yourself. Our Unification Church must also abandon a lifestyle centered solely on the Unification Church. This is because we are all cells and molecules of the universe.

In these end times, we must feel the historical actions and the providential actions of heavenly principles, and we must feel the overall actions of God's love. And you must establish your body to become victors in the battle against universal Satan, so that you can become necessary beings for the garden of heaven, and at that time, heaven will have a relationship with you. To fulfill this one hope, Jesus Christ came and went, and to accomplish this hope, the Trinity of God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit is united in fighting against Satan.

When you try to fight against Satan today, you must discern whether the thoughts, concepts, or all your intentions are for yourself or not. If you think everything is for yourself, you will have no way to escape the realm of Satan.

And we Christians who are moving towards the world must transcend the historical consciousness within the world. We must become people who can grasp and feel the world with a universal historical consciousness.

Blessed are the peacemakers
So what will the world for restoration be like? What will society for restoration, family for restoration, and I for restoration be like? What is God's will for restoration? You must become someone who knows and transcends all of this. To do so, you must live relying on the word, have the serving heart of Jesus Christ, and be able to bring harmony among each other. Jesus said, "Blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called the children of God." (Matt 5:9)

Wherever you go, a person who can bring peace can draw near to God. You have the responsibility to bring peace to every individual, the responsibility to bring peace to all nations, the responsibility to bring peace to the world, and the responsibility to bring peace between heaven and earth.

If you do not feel this practical responsibility in the living environment you are in, you must feel it in your heart at least. You must have the heart to become a sacrifice that can bring peace to individuals, families, societies, nations, and the entire world. Thus, you must become someone who can stand before the Father in opposition to Satan.

If you live in such a relationship, when you see someone doing good, you will feel the desire to bow your head and elevate them. And when you see someone doing bad, you will feel that guiding that person is my responsibility. If there is someone who lives with such realizations, they do not need to pray for their own individual needs. They do not need to pray for their family. Each of you must make a resolution and oath to build the heaven that God desires on this earth, and if you live for that, God will be with you.

Therefore, if there is a nation that can hold hands and build an altar of peace, that nation will bring about a continuous new revolution towards the world. The church will also be the same. If there are those who can hold hands and, following the example of Christ, become sacrifices for peace, even if their steps may seem unlikely to succeed or may seem to break, that is not the case. Their steps are firm steps towards the construction of the heavenly kingdom on earth.

Jesus Christ came to this earth bearing the amazing mission of heaven and earth. In the 4,000-year historical process, when there were no loyal subjects for heaven and no filial piety for heaven, Jesus Christ came to fulfill the mission of a loyal subject and a filial child that heaven required.

The life of Jesus for over thirty years was a life for heaven. It was a global and universal life. Moreover, His life was a sacrificial life for heaven. Therefore, you must follow Jesus Christ, who came as a filial child for heaven, a being that has never existed in history.

The will of the Father is to establish heaven. What is heaven? It is a world where all humanity holds hands, harmonizes, lives in mutual peace, and lifts their hands in glory and gratitude before heaven. When you think of this, the faith life we have lived today has been a very childish faith life. Now we must settle that childish faith life.

God who aims for the ideology of unification
Now the era of denominationalism has passed. The era of nationalism has also passed. Now is the time when we must seek a universal ideology of restoration and a universal ideology of faith.

Today, the Korean people are a pitiful nation. What this pitiful people must understand is that God's history breaks down the individual to establish the family, breaks down the family to establish society, breaks down society to establish the nation, and breaks down the nation to find and establish the world. This is the judgment of heaven.

Humanity has gone through such judgment, but what is the final issue that remains? It is to completely break the Cain line that has fought against Abel. Therefore, you must become a different person centered on the words of Jesus. You must establish the words of Jesus as the law and become a different person. You must all become loyal subjects and filial children of heaven who substitute for the life of Jesus.

Thus, you must come before God, who aims for the ideology of unification, and say, "God, please resolve the resentment that you have not been able to unify the world into one and love it until now through me."

However, today Christians do not realize that they have such a historical, universal, and cosmic mission before them.

So how much have you manifested the love of Jesus Christ today? To what extent have you equipped yourselves with faith and life through Jesus? You must know that boundary line.

The grace that comes through Jesus is universal grace. Therefore, today we must live with the consciousness of heaven. In all your actions, and even in all your feelings today, you must have the centered heart of "I am the representative of heaven" and live with that concept.

Even when you are scolded by all people and feel angry, you must suppress that anger with the realization that your one anger will cause 2.4 billion humanity to be scolded. Heaven has been coming with such feelings until now. If you know this and still become angry and act against God's will, what will happen? All members must unite and cooperate with each other.

Is there someone in difficulty? You must feel that person's difficulty as if it were a wound on your own body. And you must cooperate. This cannot be done only by the Korean people. All humanity must cooperate.

You must walk the path for the return to heaven. You must become sons and daughters who live receiving the love of the Heavenly Parent. After that, you must be able to host God, who is the center of the Heavenly Parent. The God you are calling out to, the Jesus Christ you are seeking and believing in, is not just God for you, nor is Jesus Christ just for you. However, today, those who believe in Jesus do not know this. They only know Jesus and God as being for themselves.

But that is not God's hope. That is not God's will. God's position is the center of all heaven and earth. Today, you must know how to host God in that way. However, this will only be possible for those who live a heavenly life.

Correct faith in God
So why has God been guiding the history of 6,000 years? It is to embrace the entire history in His one bosom. He is the God who wishes for not only the earth but also the spirit world to become one in His love and has longed for that day. If you wish to receive grace before such a God, you must pray, "Father! Please call me."

God's love must not stop with you. Today, you must understand that the gifts given by heaven are not just for you.
It is for saving you while simultaneously saving all of humanity.  
However, today, since humans live centered around themselves, many people wish to seek God, but there are very few who have received grace.  
Today, we must break free from this. We must penetrate and break through this to welcome the universal God as the universal God. We cannot help but feel a profound responsibility before such a cosmic God.  

**The Chosen People for the Restoration of Heaven**  
The garden of hope that you believe in and desire is not just your own garden of hope. The archangel fell because he tried to seek and believe in God centered on himself.  
The God that humanity believes in today is my God, and at the same time, He is the God of all humanity. He is our God, and at the same time, He is a global God; He is a global God, and at the same time, He is the God of heaven and earth. He is also the cosmic parent.  
However, when we look at the faith of those who believe in Jesus today, they are saying, "Be my God." And a little further, they are saying, "Be the God of my family." When we go a little higher, they say, "Be the God of our denomination." We must not have such notions.  
Today, there are many denominations that cry out to God in the world. However, the God who is called upon within the denominational circles is no longer needed. We must gather those who can believe and call upon that one existence, transcending denominations, as my Father, representing the whole. Only such beings can host God on this earth.  
Therefore, today, we must relate the concept that we feel to the whole through our families. You who have entered a new path must now abandon your past life and make a new historical start toward a cosmic life concept.  
At such a time, what kind of heart should you have? You must have a heart that can host the existence of the cosmic God. Thus, you can receive God's love and establish a relationship where you can give and take with God. Only then can you conclude the ideal of the cosmic bride.  
After concluding the ideal of the cosmic bride, you can seek the restored world. However, I can only appear as a bride before the existence of the cosmic God when the nations, peoples, brothers, children, and couples are restored. Only by reaching that position can I stand before the existence of the cosmic God centered on the love that has arisen from there and become one with that love. Thus, the couple that is united can govern this earth and live in heaven. Moreover, only by giving birth to children as such a couple can we build a heavenly family, and only by forming a people as such brothers and children can we finally conclude the restoration providence and live the life of the heavenly kingdom on earth.  
Thus, the great movement for the restoration of heaven is being presented through you today. Therefore, you must make greater efforts to fulfill that will and must not be cowardly before Satan. Just as Jesus Christ fulfilled the duty of a loyal son for one will, we must also equip ourselves with the duty of a loyal son.  
To complete the restoration of heaven and give glory to victory,  
not only this nation but all of humanity, and furthermore, all spirits in the spirit world must be made to know how to fulfill the duty of loyalty and filial piety before heaven, so that they can be sons, children, brothers, families, or even nations that can give glory to the victory of the restoration of heaven before the Father. You must surely understand this.  

**Prayer**  
Beloved Father, today we must run. Though we lack strength, we are facing an immense historical end where we must leap over dozens of stages at once. Even though I stand in a position where I must elegantly overcome the process of judgment, today we are deeply asleep.  
Father, we are intoxicated by the secular world. We are accompanied by sin. We, who are like this, earnestly wish and hope that after clearing away all elements of evil, we can be established as victors who can give glory to the Father, the center of the universe.  
All historical circumstances are entangled in our being today; please cut them off and establish a center of liberation so that we can stand in the position of a friend of Jesus Christ and be established as a joyful being who can worship before the Father.  
Let us, the chosen ones for the restoration of heaven, not be those who live centered on ourselves while trampling on the ideals of heaven. Allow us to be led by the ideals of heaven, to go forward and forward until we achieve that ideal, to sacrifice and sacrifice, to fight and fight, and to be able to endure and win until we can host You as the cosmic Father.  
Father, please forever govern our hearts. Now, through a new cosmic standard of living, allow us to be sons and daughters who can give thanks and worship before You, the center of the whole, and who can be immersed in Your love. I earnestly request this and pray all things in Your name. Amen.  

**Selected Words of Rev. Sun Myung Moon**
